The Twists and Turns of the Hunan Army's Reduction

▲ Dai Huiyuan Disagrees with the Reduction

▲ But He Has Already Left Changde for Hankou

Yangtze River Communication: Because He Jian owes a huge amount of more than 5 million yuan in military expenses in Hunan Province, he is doing his best to reduce the army to maintain it. He previously issued a reduction order, totaling the cancellation of the 9th and 10th Independent Brigades, the Xiangxi Bandit Suppression Command, the Column Headquarters, the First and Third Bandit Suppression Battalions, and the name of Independent Regiment, which can save 100,000 to 200,000 yuan in military expenses per month. However, Dai Huiyuan, the commander of the 10th Independent Brigade and the commander of the Xiangxi Bandit Suppression, originally had two regiments under his jurisdiction, He Ying and Xiang Keqiang, and Li Guojun's Column Headquarters. This reduction, He Regiment was編制into the 16th Division's teaching regiment, Xiang Regiment was into the 31st Division's 3rd Brigade 5th Regiment, and Li's troops were into the 15th Division's 44th Brigade. Although the names have changed, their positions have not shaken. Only Dai Huiyuan alone was relieved of his duties as brigade commander and commander of the Xiangxi Bandit Suppression and transferred to be a counselor of the General Headquarters. Dai's troops are all in Fengzhou to suppress He Long. Dai himself led a special service battalion to guard Changde. On the evening of February 19, Dai suddenly led the entire special service battalion out of the west gate. On the morning of the 20th, the Changde area was greatly shocked, thinking that Dai's troops had rebelled. At the same time, Dai's command post was robbed by scattered soldiers, and officers and soldiers in Dai's troops and their families fled one after another, and order was almost disrupted. Tang Youyue, the magistrate of Changde County, Li Houkun, the director of the 19th Division's garrison office in Changde, and Hu Kun, the commander of the Changtao-Han three-county regiment defense, rushed to send regiment soldiers and standing troops to the streets to suppress them before order was maintained. At the same time, they jointly issued a notice to reassure the people, which read: "According to the report, Dai's troops have left Changde. The local government has sent standing troops and the garrison office of the 19th Division and the command of the Changtao-Han regiment defense area to be jointly responsible for maintaining the security of the city and the officials and subordinates of the department. Anyone who spreads rumors to confuse the public or infringes on the officials and subordinates of the department will be dealt with by military law once they are captured. This is hereby announced, and all must comply with it and not violate it." It was not until after 1:00 p.m. that the people's hearts began to settle down. On the same day, Magistrate Tang summoned the responsible personnel from the military, police, regiment, and other circles and held a security meeting at the county government. It was immediately resolved that (1) the county government's standing troops would be responsible for guarding the city, (2) the soldiers of the 19th Division's garrison office would be responsible for inspecting hotels and patrolling the streets, (3) any army, without orders, would not be allowed to enter the city, and (4) He General Commander would be telegraphed to rush to send troops to Changde to take over the defense. Before the troops taking over the defense arrived in Changde, Tang County Magistrate, Director Li, and Commander Hu would consult and handle matters related to security at any time. Therefore, order was slightly restored.

He Jian paid great attention to the report of Dai Huiyuan's escape. In addition to flying the entire Tao Liu Brigade of the 19th Division from Cha You to the province and transferring them to Changde by car to take over the defense, he also telegraphed various counties in Xiangxi to investigate Dai Huiyuan's whereabouts. On the 21st, he received a secret telegram from Taoyuan County, stating that Dai Huiyuan had arrived in Taoyuan, and Dai also telegraphed his troops He Ying, Xiang Keqiang, Li Guojun, and others to concentrate in Taoyuan, which was about to change, etc. According to the report, He Jian immediately issued three telegrams: (1) A circular telegram to various troops in Hunan Province, stating that those who destroy the reduction order or take extraordinary actions will be dealt with by military law. (2) A secret telegram to Li Jue, the commander of the 19th Division, Zhang Ying, the commander of the New 11th Division, and Chen Quzhen, the commander of the New 32nd Division, to strictly prevent Dai's troops from taking extraordinary actions and strictly stop them. (3) Order Tao Liu Brigade of the 19th Division to rush to Changde at night without delay. In general, everyone was deeply afraid that He Ying, Xiang Keqiang, Li Guojun, and other troops would be incited by Dai, but fortunately, He, Xiang, and Li were not moved by Dai and telegraphed to the province one after another, expressing their sincere support for the reduction order, and all took up the positions of the newly appointed brigade and regimental commanders in Fengzhou. Dai Huiyuan then said that his troops obeyed the reduction order and refused to go to Taoyuan to gather, so he could not do anything. On the 22nd, he quietly left Taoyuan and went to other places secretly. On the 23rd, Dai Hongxun, the chief of staff of the Xiangxi Bandit Suppression Command, telegraphed to He Jian from Taoyuan, saying that Dai Huiyuan had gone to Hankou for medical treatment due to illness, and the special service battalion under his command was waiting for orders in Taoyuan, and it was proposed to return to the establishment of He Regiment, and there was no abnormal movement. The rumors about Dai in Changde were actually a misunderstanding. On the same afternoon, Taoyuan County Magistrate Ouyang telegraphed to report that Dai had left the county to go to Hankou, and the special service battalion under his command had gone to Chenzhou, and the local area was peaceful. As for the entire Tang Xinzhao Regiment of Tao Liu's troops, they arrived in Changde at noon on the 23rd to take over the defense. The twists and turns of Dai's troop reduction came to an end here. (February 24)

Wuhu Quick News

▲ After Anhui Province created levies for rice certificates and surcharges on salt by the jin (unit of weight), Anhui people repeatedly opposed them. The central government also issued telegrams to stop them. However, to raise funds for government expenses, the provincial government continued to collect them. Regarding the rice certificate levy, when officials and merchants were deadlocked, rice transported out of Wuhu by steamship was temporarily recorded by the General Auditing Office for Rice Transport by Steamship in Anhui. Recently, as the office received a telegram from the Department of Finance ordering collection according to regulations, it has now implemented the collection of a donation of four jiao per shi (unit of volume) of rice exported. As for the salt tax surcharge, it is two yuan per shi in southern Anhui and two yuan and four jiao in northern Anhui, and offices have long been established to collect them. However, after the central government abolished likin (internal transit tax), it decided to unify the salt tax, with the central government taking over the collection of salt jin surcharges from all provinces starting from March 1. It also issued a circular to all provincial governments, ordering them to comply with the arrangement of the central government allocating a certain amount of subsidies to each province on average each month based on the future collection amount. The Anhui Salt Monopoly Bureau also repeatedly received urgent requests from the Ministry of Finance to have the Audit Office take over the collection and remittance of the Anhui salt jin surcharge and the price increases for Jiangsu and Anhui, starting from March 1. To maintain the unification of the salt tax, the Anhui provincial government recently telegraphed the Salt Monopoly Bureau to comply with the ministry's order and implement the handover on the first of next month.

▲ Communist bandits in Jiangxi Province have been harassing the border of Anhui. Chen Tiaoyuan previously telegraphed the 57th Division stationed in Wuhu to dispatch the entire Third Battalion of the 341st Regiment to Yin Jia Hui to defend against them. They scattered the fleeing bandits. Now, the battalion has received orders to return to Wuhu today, leaving only one company to garrison. Furthermore, the Yu Fengrun unit of the 342nd Regiment of the division stationed in Guangde has now received orders to depart for Wuhu and then proceed to Hefei to garrison and intercept mutinous soldiers from Liu'an.

▲ Yesterday, the Wuhu Local Court escorted four bandits sentenced to death – Liu Xisan, Chen Ruilin, Deng Hongtao, and Wang Youyi – to the Beiping Road outside the Thirteen Arches to be executed by firing squad. (January 27)

Local Correspondence

Suzhou

Change of Construction Bureau Director: Wei Zumo, Director of the Wuxian Construction Bureau, has been ordered to be transferred to the position of Director of the Donghai County Construction Bureau, concurrently managing construction affairs in Ganyu and Guanyun counties. The original Director of Donghai, Jiang Tongyi, is awaiting another appointment. Qian Tianpeng, the current Director of the Shishan Construction Bureau, has been transferred to Suzhou to succeed Wei, vacating the position in Baoshan, which will be concurrently held by Wu Wenhua from Shanghai County.

Mao Naijing's Appeal Rejected: Mao Naijing, the former Chief of the Dongtai Public Security Bureau, was sentenced to two years' imprisonment and fined 1,000 yuan for dereliction of duty and fraud. He appealed to the Jiangsu High Court. The verdict was announced on the afternoon of the 28th, rejecting the appeal and upholding the original judgment.

Wuxi

Theft of Funds Leads to Suicide in Wuxi: A man named Yuan Siguan, 24 years old, was from Beikuzhen, Bachixiang, Suzhou. He had collected silver dollars at home and traveled to Suzhou to purchase embroidered goods wholesale to open a Shenpao (god robe) store in the town. After arriving in Suzhou, he stayed in Room 7 of the Yi Da Inn outside Tumeng. That night, Yuan happened to meet Shen Erguan (a 35-year-old local man) whom he had known from his time working at the Jinchangsheng store in Shengzezhen. They stayed at the inn together. Unexpectedly, the next morning, Shen Erguan, seeing that Yuan Siguan was sound asleep, stole a leather suitcase that Yuan had placed beside his pillow (containing 135 yuan in banknotes) and left. When Yuan discovered the theft, he immediately took a car to Wuxi, searching everywhere for him, but to no avail. Around 5 PM the day before yesterday, Yuan Siguan passed by the Wu family’s outhouse by the river at Lihuangni Bridge inside the Old North Gate, and suddenly had a death wish. He took off his belt from his waist and hung it on the beam of the outhouse, hanging himself. Fortunately, a passerby discovered him, took him down, and gave him first aid, gradually bringing him back to consciousness. Later, the owner of the outhouse, Wu Yushu, learned about it and, feeling sorry for Yuan Siguan, generously donated nine yuan and four jiao. Meanwhile, Gao Chongshan, the Chief of the First Public Security Sub-bureau in charge of the area, dispatched police to take Yuan to the bureau. Yesterday, Chief Gao dispatched police officers again to send Yuan back to Suzhou, handing him over to the Cangqu Public Security Sub-bureau to inform his family to come to Suzhou to take him back, to prevent further accidents.

Investigation of Nantang Boat Accident Concludes: The Houchi-class steamship of the Taili Steamboat Company capsized near Nanshuixian Temple on the 14th, resulting in the drowning of ten passengers. After the County Public Security Bureau transferred the case to the County Court, the Prosecutor's Office implemented an investigation, detaining Yang Xiangqi and two other managers of the company for interrogation. At the same time, the families of the victims organized a joint association, held meetings, and hired lawyers to pursue litigation. Now, the County Court Prosecutor's Office, based on the accusations from all parties and after interrogating Yang Xiangqi, has concluded the investigation. Yesterday, it transferred the entire case to the Trial Division to file a public prosecution. The Trial Division has also issued summonses, scheduling a hearing for February 2, and separately summoning the five bereaved families who have filed lawsuits: Mi Zhu, Yang Qiaoquan, Gu Dechang, Yang Baiquan, and Wang Longguan. In addition to hiring lawyers to file lawsuits with the County Court, the Bereaved Families Association has also submitted petitions to the Ministry of Transportation, the Provincial Government, the Department of Construction, the County Government, and the Construction Bureau, requesting relief and asking the County Party Headquarters to uphold justice and provide assistance.

Inquiries by Telegram Regarding Methods for Smuggling Rice Exports: Since the government explicitly ordered the abolition of likin, tax checkpoints in various places have long been abolished, and ships traveling back and forth have passed without obstruction. However, some unscrupulous merchants have taken advantage of the opportunity to smuggle white rice exports, causing rice prices to gradually increase. Huang Chengji, the captain of the Ninth Team of the Second Water Police District, believes that Yixing Wuxikou Hetanggang and other places under his jurisdiction are located at the junction of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, which has always been a shortcut for unscrupulous merchants to smuggle. Recently, since the abolition of tax checkpoints at various lake ports, rice ships have been exporting one after another. As there are no explicit regulations prohibiting this, he did not dare to intercept them without authorization. Yesterday, he sent a letter to the Yixing County Government and submitted a request to Mao, the District Chief of the Second District, for instructions on how to handle the matter. District Chief Mao immediately telegraphed the Civil Affairs Department to request instructions.

Changzhou

Jiangyin Riot Police Kill Bandits: Jin Qingxian, head of the Jiangyin Sixth District Security Regiment, and Yin Geng, chief of the Sixth Branch of the county’s Public Security Bureau, set out on the 26th with armed police to suppress bandits. Zhang Jinbei, a notorious bandit from the county, fled to Shuangwenkou in Weifeng Township, the Fifth District of Wujin. He was killed by the police, and his body was left on the roadside. Since that area is under the jurisdiction of Zheng Tianqiao’s Fifth Public Security Branch of Wujin, Chief Jin, and others went to the Fifth Branch to report and request transfer for official inspection. They also handed over another captured bandit, Qu Shunjin, to the Jiangyin County Government for interrogation. Zheng Liuqiao’s Fifth Public Security Branch reported the matter to the Main Bureau on the 27th, requesting the County Court for official inspection. On the morning of the 28th, Chief Prosecutor Yang Kongyi led officials to conduct the inspection for verification and processing.

Gamblers Resist Arrest and Assault Police: On the morning of the 26th, He Bin, a patrol officer from the First Sub-bureau police station outside Wuyi East Gate, reported that Zhao Boxi and others were gambling for profit at Mi Peigen's house. Around 6:00 PM, he dispatched police officers to the house, where they caught over a hundred gamblers and confiscated gambling paraphernalia. Zhao Zhaomin gathered a crowd to resist arrest and attacked the officers, injuring Patrol Chief Wan Fengwu and others. He also lost firearms and parts and stole nine bullets. Officer He reported to the Public Security Bureau in the city on the 27th.

Four Robbers Executed by Firing Squad: Zhang Peng, the concurrently acting Director of Wuyi County Police Bureau, previously received four captured robbers, Liu Yuanyuan, Ding Huafu, Chen Jinda, and Shi Haida, who confessed to committing multiple robberies. They were sentenced to death. On the morning of the 28th, County Magistrate Zhang dispatched supervisors to escort Liu Yuanyuan and the other three, verify their identities, and escort them to the execution ground to be executed by firing squad.

Qingpu

District Chief Conference Proposals: The County Government held its tenth District Chief Conference on the 23rd to discuss the following proposals: (1) County Magistrate's proposal: The household registration survey is long overdue and should be completed as soon as possible. Resolution: All registration forms must be completed and submitted by March 10. (2) County Magistrate’s proposal: The clearing of villages is about to expire; it should be completed as soon as possible. Resolution: All public and private firearms must be inspected by March 20. Doorplates and joint security systems must be completed by March 25.

Robbery Near Tailai Bridge: The home of a Zhang family near Tailai Bridge in the county's First District was suddenly attacked by five or six bandits in the middle of the night the other day. They broke down the door and robbed the family of a large amount of cash, clothing, and rice. They ordered Zhang to raise 300 yuan and threatened to report the family to the authorities. The bandits fled with their loot.

Nantong

Provincial Committee Auctions Zhang Cha's Assets as a Traitor: Zhang Cha, a native of the county, was charged with colluding with the enemy and local thugs in 1927. The Special Criminal Court requested and obtained the approval of the Provincial Government to issue an arrest warrant and confiscate all his property. Recently, Zhang Cha, in Dalian, presented a request to the provincial and central authorities to invoke the New Year's amnesty for the release of his property, but it was not approved. After deliberation, the Provincial Government decided to allocate 60% of the confiscated property to the province and 40% to the county for educational and charitable purposes. On the 27th, Zhang Fengzhou was sent from the Provincial Committee to Jinlai Tong to jointly auction off the property with County Magistrate Zhang. After investigation by the County Government, the value of the property in 1928 was estimated at 633,060 yuan. After deducting 108,605 yuan of disputed funds, the actual total was 524,455 yuan. It is still necessary to re-estimate the value this time.

Thorough Investigation of Irregularities in the Collection of Mang Cao Taxes: The personnel involved in the collection of Mang Cao taxes in Tong County were reported for irregularities. The Department of Finance instructed the County Government to send the original handling personnel to listen to the auditing, so as to thoroughly investigate whether the collected amount matched the amount remitted to the province, as the stub receipts and registers had already been sent to the province. The Bureau of Education submitted a request to the County Government to be forwarded to the province, stating that the education funds involved in the amount were substantial, requesting the Department of Finance to return the stubs for settlement. County Magistrate Zhang specially submitted a report to the province for verification.

Nine Bandits Captured and Sent to the Province for Interrogation: The Provincial Security Regiment searched and suppressed bandits in Hejiayuan, Fuan Town, capturing nine bandits, including San Zhiyan, He Lanliu, Shi Qianqun, Chen Xiaoru, Lu Qinghe, Sun Qiqing, Liu Zixi, Lu Zhaojiang, and Cui Chaoli, and sending them to the Provincial Security Office for interrogation.

Jiangyin

Court Investigation of Opium Case Concluded: The Garrison Headquarters and the County Police Team seized an opium case involving Chen Bingquan, the former patrol leader of the Twentieth Water Police Team, in the Yangtze River in August last year. A group of witnesses was sent to the Zhenjiang District Court by the county. The interrogation had been conducted several times and had not been concluded. The court held a hearing on the 25th, questioning Chen Bingquan and others. Chen stated that the opium was insufficient and asked the court for a light sentence. Pan Rongfu was then questioned: "Did Chen Bingquan order you to pick up the opium?" Pan said no. The interrogator questioned him, stating that the facts were obvious and denying them was useless. Then, Qiu Zanqing was asked: "Is the opium yours?" Qiu stated no. The interrogator said that even if the opium was not yours this time, you have also been involved in relief work before. The court concluded that the investigation of the case was now completed. They were scheduled to rule on the 27th. The three were returned to custody.

Communist Xu Hongying's Surrender Deemed Inadmissible: The County Reorganization Committee, based on Xu Hongying (Xu Zhensheng) inadvertently joining the Communist Party, requested to surrender. At yesterday's meeting, it was found that Xu's case did not meet the legal requirements for Communists surrendering. The request was deemed inadmissible. Also, the Communist Chen submitted a request stating that he was innocently arrested, pleading for the case to be dropped and to be spared from injustice. How should this be handled? It was resolved that the case was a criminal matter, and the committee was not in a position to accept it. He was instructed to appeal to the County Government.

Detective Zhang Wenlang Assassinated: Zhang Wenlang, from Zhangjiagang, Houteng, was originally a bandit. He surrendered while serving as the leader of the Huang Detective Team in the past year and was made a detective. He was usually in the countryside. Around 8:00 PM the other day (26th), he was drinking tea in a tea shop in Sanxingzhen when a group of bandits suddenly pulled out pistols and shot him, hitting a vital point and killing him. The town leader of the town, Liu Changru, immediately reported to the district office, which forwarded the report to the county for official inspection.

Zhenjiang

Director of Xicheng Construction Bureau Transferred: The Jiangsu Construction Department announced yesterday that Yao Dixing, Director of the Wuxi Construction Bureau, was transferred to the position of Director of the Jiangyin Construction Bureau. Mao Fengze, the original Director of the Jiangyin Construction Bureau, was transferred to the position of Director of the Wuxi Construction Bureau.

Correction of Names for Long-Distance Telephone Numbers in Various Counties: The Department of Construction, based on a report from Deng Fupei, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Electricity Management Office, stated that the names of county-owned long-distance telephones in various counties were inconsistent and could easily cause misunderstandings. The Department heard that in addition to changing the names to "County Town Rural Telephone of [County Name]" and filing a report with the government for record, and instructing for notification, they specially notified the county magistrates, the Construction Bureau, and the Construction Office of each county yesterday to be aware.

Change of Standing Committee Member of County Party Headquarters: Wu Lianqing, a standing committee member of the County Party Headquarters Executive Committee in this county, resigned due to personal matters. The committee approved his resignation at a standing committee meeting and elected Jing Nian to succeed him.

Clearing Village Headquarters Approves Bandit Surrender: The Jiangsu Clearing Village Headquarters believes that among the bandits in various counties, many were wrongly induced or coerced. If they were not allowed to surrender, they would never have a chance to reform. Therefore, in accordance with Article 17 of the Clearing Village Regulations, it drafted nine articles of interim measures for handling bandit surrenders in Jiangsu Province. It requested the Provincial Government to discuss them. The Provincial Government presented them to the 372nd meeting, which resolved to approve them, consult the Pacification and Supervision Office for joint issuance, and report them to the headquarters for record. Therefore, the Clearing Village Headquarters specially notified the Clearing Village Bureaus of various counties yesterday to instruct all Clearing Village Sub-bureaus to follow them accordingly.

Rugao

The Smuggling Suppression Camp Reorganized into an Army Battalion: The Rugao Smuggling Suppression Camp was ordered yesterday by the Smuggling Suppression Headquarters to be reorganized into the Second Battalion of the Army. Furthermore, the Smuggling Suppression Camp's salaries, which were previously issued by the Inspection Office, were ordered yesterday by the Inspection Office to be claimed from the Rugao Juegang Tax Bureau. Battalion Commander Zhu has already sent the roster to Juegang for verification.

Three Accomplices of Bandits Apprehended: Chen Changli, Feng Jinsheng, and Wu Chunyang, accomplices of bandits in Nankan, were arrested by the Coastal Defense Regiment for providing food to the bandits and arranging ransom negotiations. The three accomplices have been sent to the Central Team Headquarters for strict handling according to the law.

Fengxian

Prohibition of Political Police Extorting Money from Gambling and Opium Dens: County Magistrate Shen Qingchen discovered that some lawless political police were using the pretext of secretly investigating gambling and opium dens to extort money outside. Therefore, in addition to issuing a public notice prohibiting this yesterday, he also stipulated the following measures: (1) All reports of opium addicts or private opium sellers, as well as substitutes and all criminal offenders, must be signed and sealed by the reporter and include their place of origin and occupation, and have a reliable shop guarantee; otherwise, they will not be accepted. (2) The political police handling the case must wear badges and be issued official credentials by the County Government. Anyone falsely using the name or extorting money will be allowed to be arrested and reported for punishment. All fines for gambling and opium dens will have official approvals and will be announced and published at the end of the month. If there is any embezzlement or omission, it can be reported to the County Government to ensure accuracy.

Divorced Daughter-in-Law Leaves, Son Returns to His Clan: Zhang Qing, a farmer from the 39th Tu of the Eighth District, had no son. Seven years ago, he recruited Ruan Dasheng from the same Tu to marry his eldest daughter, Baoyun, to continue his lineage. However, after the marriage, the daughter suddenly disliked her husband's appearance and firmly refused. Zhang was forced to marry Chen Qiaozhen, the daughter of Chen Yuan from the 40th Tu, as a substitute. She was married in the first month of last year. At that time, Dasheng showed no dissent on the surface, but since his wife was not his original spouse, he harbored resentment in his heart, leading to conflicts in the family. Since Zhang Qing himself now had a biological son, his treatment of Dasheng became increasingly poor, leading to a widening gap between the two parties. Now, Dasheng's new wife has fled due to abuse from her parents-in-law. At the same time, Dasheng wants to divorce her. Therefore, on the 28th of last month, relatives and friends gathered the two parties for negotiation. An agreement was reached that they would separate. Zhang Qing was responsible for finding another wife for Dasheng. Dasheng suddenly indicated that he would not recognize anyone except his original wife’s biological daughter. Since Zhang's daughter had already been married off, the clan mediated again. As a result, since Dasheng did not want to take the surname, he drew up an agreement yesterday to return to his own clan. In addition, Zhang posted 80 yuan as expenses for returning home and completing the marriage.

Xiaoshan

Smuggling Suppression Soldiers Smash Public Security Sub-bureau: On the afternoon of the 24th, soldiers from the Smuggling Suppression Camp stationed in Wenyan were arrested by police from the Wenyan Public Security Sub-bureau for gambling. Unexpectedly, the soldiers refused to accept this and used the entire camp to directly enter the Public Security Sub-bureau, destroying all the desks, chairs, beds, furniture, doors, and windows in the bureau. The local scholars mediated unsuccessfully. Director Du Weiguo immediately reported the incident to the County Public Security Bureau. Yesterday, a large number of police officers were dispatched to investigate. The soldier Wang Xianzeng was taken to the county for interrogation.

Hefei

The Devastation of the Liuan Mutiny: It is said that the troops of a certain division stationed in Liuan Gui'an were instigated by bandits and communists to mutiny on the 28th of the last month of the year. They first rushed into the chamber of the battalion commander and firmly requested two months' salary. The battalion commander replied that the authorities had only issued one month's salary and that if they wanted two months, he would have to borrow from the local government. The mutineers refused and shot the battalion commander, wounding the brigade commander. They then dispersed to loot along the streets. None of the homes of middle-class people or above were spared. The goods in the shoe and sock stores were completely taken by the mutineers. The looting lasted for a day and a night. It was not until the eve of the new year that they bundled up their stolen goods and fled out of the west gate towards Jinjiazai. Afterwards, the four major teams of the Liuan Security Regiment - Yang Songshan, Liu Xiushan, Zhu Menggong, and Quan Liting - maintained order. Fearing that the mutineers would return, they kept the city gates tightly closed. They were not opened until four days after the Spring Festival. It is said that Liuan has been broken into by bandits and communists three times. This is the fourth devastation.

Letters

Letter from the Relief Committee of Xiushui County

Yesterday, I read in the "Important Telegrams" section of your newspaper on February 10, a special dispatch from Changsha on the 8th, stating that there were bandits in the Manjiang Shankou area of Xiushui County, Jiangxi Province, numbering about 3,000 and claiming to be 5,000, attempting to attack Xiushui City. On the 5th, our teacher Hao Mengling gave them a head-on blow, killing many bandits and capturing a large amount of supplies. The remnants of the bandits are fleeing towards the Manjiang Shankou area and are being pursued. We were very surprised. The bandits are still entrenched in the Manjiang Shankou, Jinglin, Gongjingkeng, and Zizhuang areas of our county. Our county is sending telegrams to the authorities to request additional troops to suppress them. The rumors published in your newspaper are untrue. We are afraid that the authorities will not understand the truth and it will affect the reinforcements, causing considerable harm. We are writing to request a correction. Respectfully, Xiushui County Relief Committee, February 21.

Letter from the Capital Police Department

We are writing to you regarding the news in the newspapers of the 26th of this month about the Capital Police Department arresting officials of the Party Headquarters, which is inconsistent with the facts. In this instance, our department was following secret orders to arrest Liu Jihan and others. We only sent two or three plainclothes officers. They were not uniformed detectives, nor did they carry shackles or ropes. Furthermore, the arrests took place on the road and did not intrude into the house. They did not take place in a meeting place. We also had an official letter prepared to be sent to the Nanjing Special City Party Headquarters for investigation and assistance. This can be verified. Our department handled this case with extreme care, fearing that there would be misunderstandings from the outside world or damage to the dignity of the party. Therefore, the procedures were unusually cautious. Please disclose this to clarify the truth and publicize the facts. With respect, Capital Police Department, February 27.

Letter from Du Qiaosheng

We are writing to you regarding a news report on February 23, that the prosecutor of the Nantong County Court abandoned his post and left Nantong. This is inconsistent with the facts. In 1928, Qiaosheng was appointed as the president of the Qufu County Court in Shandong Province. At the time of the handover, a conflict occurred with his successor, Wang Yinpu, who reported him to the Shandong High Court, accusing him of failing to affix stamp duty. The Ministry was asked to investigate thoroughly. Therefore, on February 16 of this year, Qiaosheng voluntarily requested the Jiangsu High Court to temporarily suspend him from his position as prosecutor of the Nantong County Court in order to go to Beijing to defend himself before the Ministry. This was not an abandonment of his post. Fearing that this would confuse the public, I am writing to request a correction. Please publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section of your newspaper. With gratitude, Du Qiaosheng, February 26, noon.

Local News

Shanghai Carries Out Election of People's Assembly Representatives

▲Drafting Detailed Rules of Procedure

▲Determining Election Qualifications

The Shanghai Municipal Election Office for the National People's Congress Representatives has been actively proceeding since its establishment, under the supervision of Zhang Qun. It is scheduled to start working in full tomorrow (the 2nd). The situation yesterday is recorded as follows:

▲Expanding Office Space: Supervisor Zhang Qun, Chief Secretary Fan Zhengbo, and others believe that the office is located at the former International Labour Bureau address, occupying only two rooms. They are now borrowing the remaining rooms from the Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Supervisor Zhang and others went to the Foreign Affairs Office yesterday morning around 10:00 AM to survey the site and discuss borrowing it to expand the office space. The Foreign Affairs Building is the most suitable. Director Liu has agreed to ask the Ministry for instructions. In the future, it is planned to use the Foreign Affairs Building as the election site. The room on the right side will be the office of the secretaries of each group.

▲Drafting Detailed Rules of Procedure: The detailed rules of procedure for the office were drafted by Li Dachao as a result of a discussion by the secretaries the day before yesterday. Yesterday, they had already been drafted. Secretaries Fan Zhengbo, Feng Liutang, Li Dachao, Chen Kecheng, Chen Bai, and others held a meeting at the office at 11:00 AM yesterday to discuss and decide on the details.

▲Election Qualification Issues: Regarding the election qualification issues, the election groups have already been stipulated by the election regulations. However, according to Fan Zhengbo, speaking to a reporter from the Xin Sheng News Agency, only the above-mentioned groups in this city that have been guided by the Party Headquarters and filed with the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau are qualified. If they have been guided by the Party Headquarters but have not filed with the Social Affairs Bureau, or have only filed but have not received guidance, it will not be easy to accommodate them. According to the reporter's investigation, among the public groups in this city, only the district farmers' associations have organizations. It is uncertain whether the districts will elect jointly. For example, with the Chamber of Commerce, it is uncertain whether it includes the various industry associations, and whether the various industry associations will hold separate elections. Furthermore, the central government has stipulated that the reorganization of the various groups must be completed by March 15. During this time limit, will the various groups be allowed to reorganize? The election office is carefully discussing this matter and deciding on an extremely fair and appropriate method.

Zhaohe Pension Received

▲Distributed by Yang Hu, Military Advisor to the National Government

During the Zhaohe Uprising in 1915, a total of thirteen soldiers and sailors were killed. Yang Hu, Military Advisor to the National Government, was the commander of the uprising at that time. Last year, Yang submitted a request to the National Government to commend the deceased martyrs and provide pensions to their families. The National Government approved the request. The total pension to be given was 12,800 yuan, with 5,000 yuan belonging to the Ministry of Military Affairs and 7,800 yuan belonging to the Ministry of the Navy. Yang, after consulting with Mayor Zhang Qun, advanced the funds. Yang then notified the families of the martyrs to go to Yang's residence on Huanlong Road to receive their respective shares. The names of the martyrs, the amount they should receive, and the posthumous ranks they were awarded are listed as follows: Martyrs' names: Chen Kejun and Wang Ji, both posthumously awarded the rank of Rear Admiral, each with a one-time pension of 1,500 yuan; Lu Yasheng, Wang Kai, Ye Yougui, Liu Yuanhong, Wang Dagong, and He Hanying, all posthumously awarded the rank of Rear Admiral, each with a one-time pension of 1,500 yuan; Cheng Peng, Feng Weitian, Bi Zaiteng, Jin Yiting, and Chai Zi'an, all posthumously awarded the rank of Captain, each with a pension of 1,000 yuan.

National Federation of Commerce Cables Request for Serious Negotiations with Russia

▲ Using Rubles to Redeem the Chinese Eastern Railway

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China yesterday sent telegrams to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, and Mo Dehui, the plenipotentiary representative for negotiations with Russia, stating that it had previously been ordered by the Executive Yuan to investigate the exact amount of rubles issued by Russia in China in preparation for negotiations to redeem the Chinese Eastern Railway. The federation then sent a circular telegram to chambers of commerce across the country to conduct investigations. Later, it was temporarily unable to complete the investigation on schedule. As the rubles were spread throughout the country, especially in the Northeast, merchants held them, and it was impossible to know the exact amount. The deadline had been extended several times. Later, news came that Sino-Russian negotiations had been suspended, and ticket holders paid even less attention. Shortly after, domestic military events occurred, and transportation was blocked, resulting in a delay. Since the cessation of domestic military events and the resumption of Sino-Russian conferences, the federation has again sent circular telegrams urging chambers of commerce to promptly conduct investigations. The federation has received numerous letters and telegrams from chambers of commerce and merchants across the country, requesting it to submit a serious negotiation. Now that the Sino-Russian conference is about to resume, the federation will, as soon as possible, investigate, organize, and submit a report on the exact amount of rubles in our country. It is imperative to send a telegram to your government and ministries, ordering Representative Mo to initiate serious negotiations to achieve the goal of redeeming the Chinese Eastern Railway with rubles. This is the earnest prayer of Lin Kanghou, chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, and standing committee members Su Minsheng, Zhang Yuquan, Lu Guangji, Chen Riping, Li Kuian, and Peng Chuli, respectfully.

Shen Yi Delivers a Lecture on Shanghai Public Works Administration

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works Director Shen Yi gave a lecture on "An Overview of Shanghai's Public Works Administration" at the Municipal Research Society of the YMCA on Sichuan Road yesterday. More than two hundred people attended. The key points of the speech are as follows: The Municipal Bureau of Public Works is the engineering bureau of the city. According to the Municipal Organization Law, it is responsible for civil engineering related to urban construction, as well as guiding and regulating road traffic and citizen construction. As for the content of the design, it involves building new urban areas and reorganizing old urban areas. Reorganizing old urban areas is a palliative measure, while building new urban areas is a fundamental solution. I will now give a brief report on the general situation of public works: (A) Building New Urban Areas Why do we need to build new urban areas? Because the capacity of commercial ships has gradually increased in recent years, and the draft has also deepened. We are concerned that the water volume of the Huangpu River will not be sufficient. Furthermore, the current lack of connection between land and water will inevitably make Shanghai's commercial port become outdated in the future. Therefore, the municipal government is carrying out construction in the Wusong area, on the one hand, building a central area, and on the other hand, building a new commercial port. The Wusong port has closer inbound traffic and is very deep. Even at low tide, ships can stop there. It is also connected to the Songhu Railway, making transportation more convenient. There are many open spaces around, making it easy to develop in the future. The buildings of various bureaus of the municipal government are scheduled to be laid the cornerstone on July 7th of this year, and will then be moved to the new urban area. The road system in the current central area has been planned, and the zoning has also been designated. The new commercial port is under construction. The progress of the central area can be divided into three points: (1) Implementing the acquisition of 5,000 acres of land; (2) Building trunk roads; (3) Preparing to build municipal government buildings; (B) Plan for Reorganizing Old Urban Areas: (1) Planning a citywide trunk road system to achieve overall citywide unification; (2) Straightening out roads that are not uniform in various districts; (C) Regulating citizen construction; buildings in the city that are in danger of collapsing or that do not meet sanitary standards will be ordered to be rebuilt; (D) Improving roads, such as Fangbang Road and Jishui Street, which were very narrow in the past and have now been transformed into Dongmen Road, becoming a major road in Nanshi. Roads currently planned for reorganization include Ximamen Road and Ximen Road; (E) Maintaining Old Roads: In addition to planting trees along the roads and repairing scattered roads, there is also ditch work. I remember that after a heavy rain in September of the 17th year of the Republic (1928), both the northern and southern cities were submerged in water. Due to economic reasons, the municipal government was unable to implement thorough measures. However, in the past three years, 21 kilometers of drainage pipes have been installed in Baoshan Road, Lujiabang Road, and other places. In terms of bridge engineering, more than forty bridges have been built on Wusong Zhongshan Road and other places. There are sixteen docks, and other public buildings include small vegetable markets, police stations, and slaughterhouses. Projects under planning include concert halls and parks. Other reportable items include significant progress in the construction industry, for three reasons: (1) The publication of construction regulations in July of the 17th year of the Republic (1928); (2) The registration of construction companies and architects; (3) The solicitation of blueprints for rental housing. The Bureau of Public Works spends 58,800 yuan per month, with only 35,000 yuan remaining for construction after deducting salaries for staff and other expenses. In terms of area, the Chinese area is 22 times larger than the Public Concession and 56 times larger than the French Concession, but in terms of funding, it is only one-thirteenth of the Public Concession and one-fifth of the French Concession. Therefore, we can only select the most important ones and implement them first. I will now present the content and organization of the Bureau of Public Works to everyone. The organization of the Bureau of Public Works is divided into five sections: (1) General Affairs Section; (2) Bridge Section; (3) Road Section; (4) Construction Section; (5) Planning Section. The bureau holds a design meeting every two weeks and a bureau affairs meeting every Tuesday to report on the handling of public works during the week.

The Social Bureau Freely Distributes Seedlings

Two Thousand Superior Seedlings

The Municipal Social Bureau purchased a large number of seedlings during last year's Afforestation Propaganda Week and distributed them to various sectors for planting, with excellent results. It is reported that the bureau will again select and purchase 20,000 superior seedlings for this year's Afforestation Propaganda Week, distributing them to various agencies and organizations in the city, as well as members of the public who are interested in planting trees. The allocation is limited to a maximum of 500 seedlings per district and a maximum of 100 seedlings per school or organization. The remainder will be allocated to the public as appropriate. After verification, they can go to the bureau between 9 AM and 5 PM on March 11 to collect the seedlings, which will be issued free of charge.

New Developments in North China Shipping

▲ Beining Plans Intermodal Transportation The products from the three northeastern provinces that are transported to inland areas are mostly soybeans, soybean oil, hides, and medicinal materials. In recent years, since the South Manchuria Railway has expanded its affiliated Dalian Steamship Company, the number of ships has increased daily, and the shipping routes have expanded. There are dedicated ships to Shanghai, Qingdao, Shantou, Hankou, Xiamen, and Guangdong, utilizing intermodal transportation to monopolize the transportation of miscellaneous grains from the eastern provinces. The transportation fees taken by the Japanese each year are very large. In order to develop the export of local products from the eastern provinces and to break the Japanese monopoly on intermodal transportation, the Beining Railway Authority is now establishing a port warehouse in Qinhuangdao for the export of goods from the eastern provinces and is consulting with Kai Luan Company (because Kai Luan in Qinhuangdao has docks, warehouses, and ships) to request that it send several more commercial ships to the port to open routes to Shantou, Xiamen, and Guangdong to carry the export goods from the Beining Railway. It will also expand the existing Shanghai route at the same time. This matter is currently being discussed. Once Huludao is developed into a free port in the future, the Beining Railway will plan to establish its own Shanghai, Hankou, Shantou, and Guangdong routes. The Japanese were shocked to hear this news, and the South Manchuria Railway Authority is paying great attention to it.

▲ Shanghai-Tianjin Chinese Ships Resume Service After the Bohai Sea was frozen last winter, Shanghai's Chinese ships stopped sailing to the Bohai Sea. They were planning to resume service last month, but Tianjin experienced a second cold snap, and the Haihe River froze again. The suspension of Chinese ships from Shanghai to the Bohai Sea lasted for more than two months. Now that the weather is gradually warming and the number of goods shipped from Shanghai to Tianjin is increasing, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is planning to resume Bohai Sea shipping services and telegraphed Tianjin to inquire. Yesterday, they received a reply stating that the ice on the Haihe River has melted, the temperature is 40 degrees, and ships can pass. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has decided to resume Bohai Sea shipping services starting March 3 and has assigned the Xinfeng ship for the first run.

▲ Chinese Ships Begin Sailing to Weihaiwei Weihaiwei has long been under British occupation, and no Chinese ships have sailed there. Since the National Government recovered the port last year and organized an administrative bureau to handle government affairs, Director Xu requested that the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company open a shipping route to Weihaiwei to facilitate commercial transportation and promote municipal prosperity. At the same time, the British merchant Taikoo ships stopped sailing. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company telegraphed the Ministry of Communications requesting an allocation of 4,000 yuan for the start-up costs of establishing a branch office. It also ordered the Yantai branch manager to go to Weihaiwei to prepare for the establishment of an office, waiting for the ice to thaw before officially opening the route. This matter has been planned for more than three months. Now that everything is ready, they are waiting for the Ministry of Communications to allocate the subsidy before opening the route. Yesterday, the bureau also submitted the budget for the establishment of the Weihaiwei bureau and the operating expenses for the shipping route to the Ministry of Communications. It was originally planned to open the maiden voyage on March 3, but the Ministry of Communications' approval has not arrived, so it has been decided to postpone it for one more run, about ten days. The Weihaiwei route will be implemented on the next voyage of the Xinfeng ship.

The Foreign Concession Water Company Extra-Collects Water Fees

▲ Real Estate Association Writes to British Consul to Legally Stop the Practice

The Shanghai Real Estate Association wrote to British Consul-General Sir John Brenan yesterday, stating: "Dear Sir, According to a letter from member Xinping Company, water fees are usually included in the gross rent. For example, if the water fee is 6% of every 100 yuan of rent, then the net rent is 94 yuan and 34 cents, and the water fee is 5 yuan and 66 cents. The British-owned Shanghai Waterworks Company collects water fees not based on the net rent approved by the Municipal Council, but based on the gross rent. This kind of unjust enrichment by the company and the landlord's meaningless loss totals two to three hundred thousand yuan annually, which should be corrected as soon as possible. Although our company's contract with the water company stipulates a certain water fee and does not send a bill report, this certain water fee was previously calculated based on the gross rent and was requested by the water company, and it was also allowed to deduct the rent for vacant houses. In order to recover this meaningless loss, that is, the loss of paying water fees on water fees, we once negotiated with the water company, and the company then issued a notice of water cut-off. For the sake of the residents' life safety, our company paid the money under duress and protest, retaining ownership of the money, which should not be paid to the water company according to law and reason. Then, we calculated the rent by deducting the water fee from the gross rent and submitted the bill to the water company. The company insisted on sophistry, and in the end, it still threatened to cut off the water supply to tenants, intending to continue to achieve the purpose of obtaining other people's property by violent and coercive means. The company is so domineering, seeking illegal benefits. Not only is our company's rights being plundered, but all landlords will be exploited by it. Now our company no longer needs to respond to the company's final threatening letter, but only to copy the correspondence and send it to your association for verification, and quickly negotiate with the British consul to stop the company's illegal and unreasonable actions and protect the legitimate rights of all our landlords, in order to maintain Sino-British commercial friendship." The last time your country's merchant-run Shanghai Waterworks Company, for the sake of adding water fees, disregarded humanity and used violent coercive means of cutting off water, almost causing a major case similar to the May Thirtieth Movement in 1925. Fortunately, those in charge mediated in many ways, and nothing happened. Now, the member is arguing over the fact that water fees should not be collected again on water fees, which is an act of protecting legal rights and a very fair method. If the water company believes it is inappropriate, it has the legal procedure to appeal to a public judgment or court. However, it does not do this, but resorts to cutting off the water supply at every turn as a threat, and even vents its anger on residents instead of confronting those who are arguing, which is even more inhumane. This kind of behavior, which is similar to using violent coercive means and intends to continue to obtain other people's property, is likely to cause major misunderstandings and hinder the traditionally good Sino-British commercial relationship. Our association is very concerned. According to the letter, we hereby send this letter in response, hoping that you will investigate and order the company to handle the matter in accordance with legal means, and not to collect water fees on water fees again, so as to avoid resentment and maintain the long-standing friendship in Sino-British trade. We trust in your fairness."

Ministry of Finance Disapproves the Establishment of Zhenghua Bank

▲ Insufficient Capital...Defective Articles of Association

The application of Shanghai's Zhenghua Bank for registration was previously rejected by the Ministry of Finance, stating that the submitted documents were not signed and sealed by the board of directors and supervisors, which did not comply with the regulations.

Page 14

Moreover, of the required legal documents, only the articles of association were submitted, failing to comply with the provisions of Articles 3 and 5 of the Bank Registration Regulations. The Ministry was unable to verify the documents, and the request for approval and issuance of a license was denied, and the articles of association were returned. The company then complied with the instructions, corrected the procedures, and submitted the documents again. Now, Finance Ministry Qian Yu No. 10634 has been received, stating that the submitted documents and attachments have been reviewed. Although there is no fixed amount of capital required according to the current regulations, a small fixed amount would result in an unstable operating foundation. Shanghai is a prosperous commercial area, and banking operations require substantial capital to operate smoothly. The company's total capital is only 100,000 yuan, and according to the regulations, only 50,000 yuan is collected, which is too little. Since the company is established by raising shares, it should also establish a prospectus in accordance with the regulations and submit it for approval. Furthermore, the submitted articles of association are also incomplete, and the registration request cannot be approved. The attached documents are returned. This is the approval.

Gaoqiao Township Residents Oppose Foreign Merchants Building Oil Tanks

Since the wave of building oil tanks by the Asia Oil Company subsided in Gaoqiao Township (i.e., Laoshu Sha) in Songnan, another foreign merchant, Texaco, has been encircling land and starting construction to build oil tanks. Five Thousand Yuan in Taxes Stolen from a Lighter in Wuhu

▲ Li Zhonggong Strongly Advocates Investigation

▲ Wuhu China Bank Expresses Satisfaction

Five thousand yuan in taxes from Datong China Bank was stolen while being transported to Wuhu. The details of this matter are reported as follows:

▲ Taxes Transported to Wuhu Five thousand yuan in salt taxes from Datong China Bank was loaded for collection by Wuhu China Bank. The money was packed in a box and handed over to the Jiangyu ship for transportation. The Jiangyu crew members were very careful in transporting the money. When they arrived in Wuhu, because no one from China Bank came to pick it up, it was handed over to a Wuhu lighter for safekeeping, and a receipt was obtained. With the procedures completed, the ship left for other destinations.

▲ Only an Empty Box Remains The next day, when Wuhu China Bank sent someone to the lighter to retrieve the money, only an empty box was left. The five thousand yuan in cash had disappeared. The person retrieving the money questioned the lighter's cashier, who said that the entire amount had been stolen and that they did not know who had stolen it. However, the cashier promised to be responsible for urgently investigating the matter in order to find out the truth.

▲ Reward for Information At that time, Wuhu lighter, in order to clarify the matter and maintain its reputation and credit due to the theft of a large sum of money, issued a reward notice and published it in the Anhui Jiang and Wuhu newspapers, offering a reward for information. The manager of Wuhu China Bank also went to the lighter and asked Li Shounong of the China Merchants Branch about it. Li said that there was no bill of lading for the transportation of the money, and according to regulations, the bureau had no obligation to be responsible. However, he personally ordered the lighter staff to be responsible for compensation.

▲ Bureau Investigates The matter was reported to the head office of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and Chief Manager Li was very angry, stating that whether there was a bill of lading or not, the theft from the lighter was due to the negligence of the staff and the dereliction of duty of the lighter's person in charge. Moreover, goods from both Anhui and Tongzhou were transported to Wuhu with bills of lading, so how could this be used as an excuse? In order to protect the rights of the shipper and ensure the safety of the transporter, even if it was stolen, it should be responsible for recovering it. He has telegraphed the Wuhu bureau, ordering it to hold the responsible person in charge of the lighter fully responsible and to recover the money, and not to allow the shipper to lose a single penny. Otherwise, the responsible persons in charge should be held liable for compensation. At the same time, in accordance with this intention, he replied to China Bank, stating that it was under strict investigation. It is reported that Wuhu China Bank expressed great satisfaction with Chief Manager Li's effective measures.

Continued News of the Gonghe Steamer Tea Room Dispute

▲ The Case Should Be Heard by the Wuhu Court

The Gonghe steamer's old and new tea room dispute has been reported in this newspaper twice. The following is a report of the news obtained yesterday:

▲ Yih Ho Foreign Firm's Claim: Yih Ho Foreign Firm, in order to eliminate future disputes, has proposed that the Yangtze River steamer tea rooms be reformed with a new method, directly employing workers and paying wages internally, not managed by the comprador. Monthly wages would be given, and the income from passenger alcohol sales would be deposited into the company's accounts, with a certain amount allocated to the tea room staff. However, when hiring, members of the guild would still be employed, but the guild has expressed its disagreement.

▲ Five Tea Room Staff Examined for Injuries: The old tea room staff members who were beaten, including Cui Wanxi, Yang Guisheng, Song Dingxun, Lin Shaozhi, and others, were sent to the court by the hospital yesterday to request an examination of their injuries, in order to obtain official injury certificates as a basis for suing Shen Shanting.

▲ Telegram Requesting Military and Police Protection: Yesterday, the Seamen's Guild, deeply concerned that the tea room staff working on the Gonghe steamer would be beaten again like in Wuhu while traveling through various ports from Shanghai to Hankou, sent telegrams yesterday to the military and police authorities in Zhenjiang, Nanjing, Wuhu, Jiujiang, and Hankou, requesting that they protect the safety of the tea room staff on board the ship at all times when the ship arrives.

▲ Number of New Tea Room Staff to Be Retained: According to Shen Shanting's proposal, in addition to retaining the old tea room staff on board, at least thirty new tea room staff members must be brought on board to work. However, the guild has not yet expressed agreement on this matter. While retaining new tea room staff is acceptable, the number still needs to be considered, it is said.

▲ Lawsuit Must Be Filed in Wuhu: The District Court Prosecutor's Office believes that since this case was first accepted by the Wuhu District Court, it should be handled by Wuhu according to Article 19 of the Criminal Procedure Law. It was ordered in court that the lawsuit should be filed in Wuhu. The group of people subsequently apprehended by the water patrol police were sent back to the court at the place where the incident occurred yesterday for trial.

Negotiations Regarding a Vietnamese Policeman Injuring a Worker

▲ French Concession Police Allow Four Things

Around 1 PM the day before yesterday, a Vietnamese policeman from the French Concession's Dazimingzhong police station, transporting many French soldiers, drove a cargo truck to Gaochang Temple in Nanshi. Unexpectedly, while passing near Guan Bridge, he suddenly knocked down a worker, Jiang Along, to the ground. A policeman from the First District Public Security Bureau immediately apprehended the Vietnamese policeman and took him to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation. Yesterday, the responsible French Concession police station immediately requested the Public Security Bureau to extradite him. However, the Public Security Bureau, believing that the Vietnamese policeman drove carelessly and injured a worker, required the French Concession police station to agree to four things: (1) bear the medical expenses of the injured worker; (2) compensate for all losses; (3) provide full compensation if the injured worker dies or becomes disabled due to the injury; and (4) punish the Vietnamese policeman who caused the accident and submit the judgment to the Public Security Bureau for review. The responsible police station agreed to all of these, and then the extradition was approved, it is said.

Social Affairs Bureau Stipulates Form of Election Ballot for Trade Union Officials

The Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau issued a notice yesterday to the preparatory committees of various industry trade unions, stating that, in compliance with regulations, the election of officers of people's organizations must use election ballots formulated by the organizations themselves. Since the reorganization of the various trade unions in the city, they are about to be established, and most of the election ballots to be used for electing officers have not been formulated. If formats are not stipulated in advance, they will inevitably be inconsistent. It is appropriate to formulate the size and format of the election ballots for the directors and supervisors of trade unions, and issue them to the preparatory committees of the various trade unions, instructing them to comply with them and print them according to the format as soon as possible (mimeograph or letterpress printing is acceptable) for use. This order includes the following dimensions and formats for the election ballots of trade union directors and supervisors: The director election ballot is 14 cm long and 10 cm wide, with the name of the candidate and the name and date of the voter noted inside. The supervisor election ballot is 14 cm long and 8 cm wide, with the same content as the director ballot.

Public Security Bureau Renovates Detention Center

▲ Construction to Begin in One Week, to Be Completed in One Month

Since Chen Xizeng took office as the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, he has been quite active in matters that should be promoted and reformed. According to Huang Daolin, the chief of the Judicial Affairs Section of the bureau, the Public Security Bureau is responsible for protecting the people. The bureau's detention center, inherited from the former Police Department, is narrow inside, and men and women are not separated. This is not only detrimental to hygiene but also unsightly. During the hot summer months, prisoners are prone to illness. The renovation has been proposed by himself, and the blueprint has been drawn. The estimated cost is around 1,000 yuan. Construction will begin in one week and is expected to be completed in one month. The interior has been divided into five sections: (1) detention center, (2) solitary confinement room, (3) holding cell, divided into ordinary and special sections, (4) guard booth, and (5) prisoner reception room. Director Chen has ordered that the renovation begin as soon as possible.

First Board of Directors and Supervisors of the Beijing-Shanghai Section of the Railway Workers' Union Took Office Yesterday

The first board of directors and supervisors of the Beijing-Shanghai Section of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Workers' Union held an oath-taking ceremony yesterday morning at 10:00 AM. First, Chairman Zou Kejian reported on the past work of the Railway Workers' Union. Due to environmental factors and the inability of members to deeply understand the union's purpose, it had fallen into disarray and even stalled. Later, the central government, in view of the fact that the Beijing-Shanghai Railway workers had made many contributions when the revolutionary army first established Jiangnan, and that it was a pity that there was no formal organization to unite them, specially appointed eleven organizing committee members to organize it. Thus, the Organizing Committee was established. Now that the reorganization work is complete, the formal directors and supervisors have also been produced. The reason why the past Railway Workers' Union stalled was because members lacked training. Therefore, future work should focus on member training to avoid repeating the same mistakes. Then, the oath-taking ceremony was held, led by representatives from the two railway special party departments and the two railway labor reorganization committees, as well as speeches from guests. After the meeting, photos were taken, and it was past 12:00 PM.

High Price of Cotton in Song City

▲ Farmers Show Joyful Expressions

The Wusong cotton market has been very prosperous recently. The six cotton firms in the town receive about 400 to 500 loads of cotton per day. The highest quality cotton can be sold for 20 yuan per load. Therefore, the villagers are all joyful. The price of green cotton has never been this high. When the new cotton was released last year, it was only sold for more than 15 yuan per load. Now it has soared by 4 to 5 yuan. According to people in the industry, the sharp rise in cotton prices is due to the influence of gold prices. Fortunately, sales are very good, and there is no accumulation. However, all farmers in the countryside who have cotton at home have already sold it all. It is expected that in the future there will be a price but no goods.
