Amidst Ten Thousand Eyes, Snow and Butterfly Confront in Court

Yesterday, they met as strangers

If I had known this day would come, why did I begin?

Hu Die demands contract termination fee of one thousand yuan

Lin says after contract termination, others can propose marriage

Lin Xuehuai deeply regrets past mistakes and still seeks reconciliation

Hu Die says the relationship is broken and it is difficult to grow old together

丨Judge advises reconciliation, adjourns for another hearing丨

The case of film star Hu Die and her fiancé Lin Xuehuai, which arose from disagreements that occurred last winter, leading to a broken engagement and subsequent lawsuit, has attracted much attention. Hu Die initially filed the lawsuit in the Shanghai District Court. Later, because the defendant resided in the Public Concession, the case was transferred to the Special District Court based on the principle of suing the defendant in their place of residence. During this period, both parties attempted reconciliation several times, but the results were unsuccessful due to significant differences in their opinions. By early February, the court had scheduled a trial date and summoned both parties to appear for the hearing. Yesterday was the date of the first hearing, and no fewer than a thousand ladies and gentlemen attended to observe, creating an unprecedented crowd. The hearing lasted for one hour, from 11:30 AM to 12:30 PM. As a result, the court ordered both parties to attempt reconciliation outside of court and adjourned the hearing until 9:00 AM on March 20. The detailed proceedings of the hearing are recorded below:

▲ Unprecedented Crowd The case was a civil lawsuit originally scheduled to be heard in the Ninth Civil Court of the court. Yesterday morning, around 8:00 AM, before the court's official opening hours, those who came to the court specifically to observe the case had already arrived in a continuous stream. The Ninth Court was already very narrow, making it difficult to accommodate even a hundred people. Therefore, in an instant, it became overcrowded, and the long corridor outside the court was also packed tightly. Those who arrived later continued to come in an endless stream. Suddenly, with a crash, one of the glass panes on the door of the Ninth Court was shattered by the crowd. The door used by the judge of the court was also broken by the crowd. The judge presiding over the case, Zhou Daren, upon learning of this situation, felt that the observers were not adhering to the courtroom's observation rules. However, since the case was being heard in public, he could not prohibit observation. Therefore, he had to think of another solution.

▲ Hearing Changed to Third Criminal Court Judge Zhou repeatedly tried to find a solution. It was reported that the Third Criminal Court, which handles criminal cases, had few cases to hear. Therefore, he decided to wait until the criminal trials in that court were finished and then transfer the case to the Third Court for hearing, as the location was very spacious and could accommodate more than a thousand people. After the news of the change of venue spread, men and women who specifically wanted to observe the hearing flooded from the Ninth Court to the Third Court like a tide. In an instant, this spacious Third Court turned into a sea of people, with shoulders rubbing against each other and heels to toes touching, breaking the new record for attendance since the establishment of the Special Court. At around 9:30, Judge Xiao Xieffen had not yet concluded the criminal case he was handling, and everyone was waiting in anticipation.

▲ Hu Die Arrives with Her Father Hu Die, the protagonist in the Snow-Butterfly lawsuit, arrived in a car with her father, Hu Shaogong, and her lawyer, Zhan Jilu, at high speed. As they stepped out of the car at the main entrance of the court, the photographers waiting in front of the door readied their equipment. Seeing Hu Die's beautiful figure gracefully passing by, they scrambled to take pictures. Although Hu Die tried to avoid them, it was too late. Hu was already slender, but yesterday she seemed to have meticulously groomed and dressed herself, making her eyebrows appear even more refined and her figure more attractive. She wore a long cheongsam with straight sauce-yellow lines and blue stripes, covered with a tiger-yellow fur coat. Her furry boots were black leather, and her stockings were flesh-colored. Holding the hem of her father's coat, she followed lawyer Zhan and walked gracefully into the Third Court through the crowd. Instantly, the atmosphere became tense, and the eyes of thousands involuntarily focused on her. However, she remained calm and sat with her elderly father in the witness seat on the left side of the courtroom, bowing her head in silence, as if deep in thought.

▲ Lin Xuehuai Arrives at Court Later Although Hu Die had arrived, Lin Xuehuai had not yet come. The observers were all looking around, and the plaintiff's representative was also in doubt. After 10:00 AM, Lin Xuehuai finally arrived at the court by car with his lawyers, E Sen and Ni. Onlookers thought that both parties were now present and that they would soon see them confront each other in court, each stating their reasons. After the judge finished hearing the criminal case and announced the adjournment, Zhou had not yet taken his seat. As a result, people talked among themselves or smoked cigarettes. In fact, at that time, Judge Zhou was hearing other civil cases in the Ninth Court and had to wait until all the cases were finished before he could go to the Third Court. Therefore, it was not until 11:30 AM that he and the clerk took their seats in the court. Upon hearing the call from the court usher, everyone in the courtroom stood up in unison to express their respect. The court usher then announced that there should be no noise in order to facilitate the hearing.

▲ Judicial Police Maintain Order However, as there were so many people, there were those who carefully maintained order, but even more who continued to talk and laugh. Furthermore, those who were standing far away, wanting to catch a glimpse of the judge's demeanor and listen to the testimonies of both parties, stood on tiptoe or stretched their necks, like watching street performers in a public square. Despite frequent waves from the court ushers urging them to sit down and listen quietly, they paid no attention to the judge's calls to maintain order. Later, police chief Hui Ding and several Western police officers came to the court and forcibly ordered the unruly observers to leave. Only then did the remaining people sit down and listen quietly, and order was maintained. This situation was even more lively than the Huang Baiying case.

▲ Today, They Are Like Strangers Hu Die sat with her father, Hu Shaogong, in the witness seat on the left. When Lin Xuehuai's lawyers arrived at the court, they initially stood in front of the lawyers' seats due to the lack of seating, repeatedly asking lawyer E Sen, "Where do I sit?" Lawyer E looked around and found no space. He then ordered someone to sit on the left side of the lawyers' seats, right next to Hu Die, only a short distance away. However, although the seats were close, they did not acknowledge each other, as if they were strangers. When they exchanged vows at the Moon Palace Ballroom three years ago, how emotional they must have been! (Hu and Lin got engaged at the Moon Palace Ballroom on North Sichuan Road on March 22, 1927. The reporter was also one of the guests at the time and took a photo, which is attached below.)

▲ Time Slips By, Hearts Suddenly Change After Judge Zhou took his seat, he first called the plaintiff, Hu Die, to ask for her name, age, origin, and address. He then asked the defendant, Lin Xuehuai, for his age and address. Then, he asked Hu Die why she was suing Lin. She replied that it was because he had requested to terminate the engagement without any reason. (Judge) Is there anything else? (Hu Die) To recover various debts totaling more than three thousand yuan, including the purchase of a car, a loan of cash, and debts owed to Hu Die's company. (Judge) What else do you request? (Hu Die) Because the defendant requested to terminate the engagement, my reputation and spirit have suffered greatly. He should be ordered to compensate for the loss of one thousand yuan. (Judge) What is the basis for this amount? (Hu Die) We have been engaged for three years. If the defendant wanted to terminate the engagement, why didn't he mention it earlier? Now, time has slipped by, and he has suddenly changed his mind. The loss is truly difficult to calculate. The amount requested now is very small, as I am afraid the defendant would not be able to afford more.

▲ Deeply Regrets Requesting Termination Judge Zhou then asked Lin Xuehuai whether he had entered into an engagement. Lin replied that the plaintiff's accusations had other intentions. The judge felt that Lin's reply was not relevant to the question, so he continued to ask whether they had entered into an engagement. Lin finally replied that the engagement was made on March 22, 1927. (Judge) Was there a matchmaker? (Lin) No matchmaker. (Judge) Was there a contract? (Lin) No contract. (Judge) Was there a betrothal gift? (Lin) There was a ring. (Judge) Is it you who wants to terminate the engagement? (Lin) I am now very sorry for the termination. Although Ms. Hu's reputation is not very good, as a film actress, social interaction is unavoidable. Therefore, I always hope to restore our original relationship. Now, I do not want to terminate the engagement. (Judge) Why did you have this idea at the time? (Lin) Because I was under too much pressure and was provoked to say this. Now, I deeply regret it, as I was in a bad environment, and there were also disreputable reports in the newspapers. (Judge) What disreputable things about the plaintiff were reported in the newspapers? Which newspaper published them? (Lin) Small newspapers (the newspaper's name is "Big Newspaper") published articles about her dancing and various disreputable things.

▲ Who Took the Initiative to Terminate the Engagement? At this time, the defendant's lawyer, Ni, stated that it was actually the plaintiff who took the initiative to terminate the engagement. The plaintiff first spoke to Zhou, then to various newspapers. The plaintiff's lawyer, Zhan Jifeng, also stated that the matter of who took the initiative will be proven in person. Judge Zhou continued to ask Hu Die when the matter of termination began. (Hu Die) Mid-December. (Judge) Did you agree? (Hu Die) Only if there were conditions, I would agree. (Judge) What kind of conditions? (Hu Die) To return the money he owed me. (Judge) How did you know about the termination? (Hu Die) He sent a letter announcing it. Lawyer Ni replied, "The termination was mentioned by the plaintiff, which was then published in the newspaper." Lawyer Zhan refuted, saying that the publication in the newspaper was later, while the defendant's letter notifying it was earlier. He then presented Lin's lawyer's first letter to Hu to the court. The judge asked Lin Xuehuai when this letter was written. (Lin) December 28. (Judge) What is the basis for saying in the letter that she had improper conduct and a sullied reputation? (Lin) It was reported in a small newspaper. I did not bring this small newspaper today. Lawyer E Sen then requested that the manager of Star Film Company, Zhou Jianyun, be summoned to the court, which could prove that the termination was actually the plaintiff's proposal. Lawyer Zhan immediately said that the defendant had already expressed his intention to terminate the engagement in writing, which was more powerful than the witness's testimony. There was no need to summon him. Judge Zhou, because the portion of the plaintiff's complaint regarding the termination was already quite clear, then changed to questioning the debt portion.

▲ Hearing of the Loan Portion First, he asked Lin Xuehuai if he owed Hu Die Company money. (Lin) Not only do I not owe it, but my salary has not been settled. However, if the plaintiff company provides evidence to prove that I owe them money, I will admit it. Now, I really don't understand. Lawyer Zhan immediately presented the bills, checks, and bankbooks to the court. The judge asked if the matter of borrowing six hundred yuan was true. (Lin) This matter was around October 4th. Hu had me cash a check to pay for the tailoring wages. In the morning, I obtained the money and gave it all to Hu at lunchtime. Lawyer Zhan said that the plaintiff could prove that after obtaining six hundred yuan that day, they also collected five hundred taels of silver at the plaintiff's place and deposited it in the Shanghai Bank branch in Hongkou, opening a current account in her name. Lawyer E Sen raised an objection, but Lin continued to say that he deposited the money in the bank on the same day for convenience and that it was not the plaintiff's money. The judge then asked about the car incident. (Lin) The contract for this car and the registration document can prove who the car belongs to. The car price was about seven hundred yuan and was purchased at the Anfei Motor Company on Avenue Albert in the French Concession. Lawyer Zhan then presented the document to the court, but stated that the money for the car was paid by Hu Die and that there was a check stub to verify this. At this time, Lawyer Ni suddenly raised a question, saying that what the plaintiff requested was the termination of the engagement and the debt. Should they order the plaintiff to state whether they wanted to terminate the engagement because of the debt? Lawyer Zhan then said that this was the power of the presiding judge and that the lawyer did not need to request it. As for the process of paying the money to the defendant, please forgive the plaintiff, as the money was generally paid by her father, and now her father is in the case and can describe it in detail. Lawyer E objected, saying that the plaintiff's father was neither a witness nor the plaintiff and objected to him representing his daughter. The judge then ordered Hu Die to report each payment date and amount given to Lin Xuehuai. Hu Die then took back the checkbook presented to the court and reported the money that Lin Xuehuai used.

▲ Report on Detailed Debt Items A total of 33 yuan and 6 jiao on April 14, 30 yuan on April 16, 50 yuan on February 19, 20 yuan on February 18, 25 yuan on June 30, 16 yuan and 5 jiao on June 15, 28 yuan and 6 jiao on July 8, 50 yuan on April 25, 50 yuan on August 29, 96 yuan and 4 jiao on November 5, 20 yuan on December 14, 50 yuan on February 27, 11 yuan on February 25, 30 yuan and 5 jiao on February 25, 37 yuan on May 13, 40 yuan on September 5, 69 yuan and 1 jiao on September 15, 100 yuan on September 29, 32 yuan and 4 jiao on October 10, 69 yuan and 1 jiao on October 12, 50 yuan on October 27, 20 yuan on October 30, 69 yuan and 1 jiao on November 15, 30 yuan on November 10, 20 yuan on April 5, 75 yuan on May 30, 20 yuan on June 29, 69 yuan on July 10, 20 yuan on August 15, 96 yuan and 4 jiao on February 5, 40 taels of standard silver on April 16, 50 taels and 9 qian and 3 fen of standard silver on October 18, 32 taels and 8 qian of standard silver on December 10, and 40 taels of standard silver on February 10.

▲ Unmarried Couple, No IOU After reporting, she continued that the above checks were all issued by the Industrial and Commercial Bank, whose head office was in Hong Kong, and this was the only branch in Shanghai. (Judge) Who signed the checks? (Hu Die) My father signed them. (Judge) Does this money belong to you or your father? (Hu Die) My father lent it to him. Lawyer Zhan then stated that Hu Die and her father were not separated. The judge continued to ask if she had any proof of the money borrowed from Star Film. (Hu Die) At that time, I had no money, so I borrowed a check from Star and paid the defendant, who said it was for speculation. After the defendant cashed the check, he went to the Shanghai Bank to open a current account in his name. Because we were an unmarried couple, it was not convenient to ask him for an IOU.

▲ Car Purchased in Installments (Judge) Who bought the car? (Hu Die) I gave him the money to buy it. The money given was also a check. Because buying a car requires a contract, and I don't know English, the defendant signed the contract. The car price was 380 taels of silver, paid in three installments. The first installment of 200 taels was a postdated check on August 30, the second installment of 90 taels was a postdated check on October 2, and the third installment of 90 taels was a postdated check on November 2, all paid to Anfei Motor Company. (Judge) Did the checks you lent to the defendant have a record? (Hu Die) Yes, but some had records and some did not.

Photo of Snow and Butterfly Engagement Poem (Taken by Jin Huating)

(Judge) How do you know that the checks without a record were used by the defendant? (Hu Die) The check stubs were annotated, so they can all be investigated. (Judge) Did you make a Western suit? (Hu Die) No, and I paid for my own clothing. Lawyer E Sen immediately stated that because they were relatives, the defendant returned 600 yuan to Hu without asking for a receipt. Now, apart from this check stub, why are there no other account books submitted to prove that Lin owed money, while the car contract and car registration document are all in Lin's name? My lawyer also went to the car sales company with Lin to investigate. However, because the car price had been paid off, the contract was lost, and the Westerner in the company was willing to provide a written statement proving that the ownership of the car definitely belonged to Lin. The plaintiff recently stated that she did not know English, so Lin signed the contract. However, there are many people in Shanghai who don't know English but buy cars. Could it be said that those who signed on their behalf can claim ownership of the purchased car? Wouldn't that be absurd?

▲ Lin Accuses Hu of Spinning Words Lin Xuehuai then stated to the court that he had an opinion to present, but he was not good with words and could not spin words like the plaintiff, which was very pleasant to listen to. He then stated that he had read the check stubs presented by the plaintiff and saw that the first item was the advertising fee for the Shishi Xinbao (China Times), from which it could be inferred that the rest was actually the plaintiff, who, because she could not resist the termination of the engagement, came up with this trick, saying that I owed her money, insulted my personality, and damaged my reputation. However, even if there was a debt, it could not be determined. However, the check stub only had the amount and date, and it could prove that the money was used by me based only on the words she wrote. The judge asked, "The plaintiff is demanding compensation of one thousand yuan because you terminated the engagement without reason. What is your opinion?" Lin replied, "I do not want to terminate the engagement now and hope to maintain the original state. However, even if the termination was due to the plaintiff, she can still be a film actress after the termination, and others can freely propose to her. What loss is there?"

▲ Hu Says Lin Values Money Over Love The judge told the plaintiff, "The defendant has now expressed that he does not want to terminate the engagement. You were friendly before, and the defendant regretted his recklessness. This court also hopes that reconciliation is the best outcome." Hu Die said, "We first became friends and then engaged. The defendant initially treated me very well, willingly doing things that others and servants were unwilling to do for me. I was very happy, so I was very willing to let him use the money I earned, and the use was also appropriate. Later, I suddenly heard people say that the defendant was actually wasting the money, drinking, whoring, gambling, and dancing, doing everything. I repeatedly advised him that my money was earned with hard work and should not be squandered arbitrarily. However, the defendant not only did not listen but also changed his gentle attitude into a violent one. I had no choice but to supervise the economy, and the defendant became even more extreme, which was really disheartening. I realized that the reason he treated me well before was not because he loved my character but because he loved my money. Friends heard about it and all advised me to leave, but I still hoped that he could repent and reform."

▲ Relationship Broken, Difficult to Grow Old Together Before long, he suddenly sent a lawyer's letter proposing to terminate the engagement. I replied asking about the conditions. He ignored me and insisted on terminating the engagement, declaring that our relationship was over. I am grateful for the court's advice to reconcile, but I feel uneasy. After we get married in the future, I fear that there will still be no good outcome. Marriage is not a child's play. Since our feelings have been broken, how can we grow old together? Therefore, I really do not want to reconcile and can only let him spread rumors. Lawyer E then defended the defendant, saying that Lin Xuehuai had previously misunderstood due to rumors. Since the plaintiff was involved in a lawsuit with a small newspaper, Lin deeply regretted his past mistakes. My lawyer also advised him to go to dance halls less often, or to go with his wife. If the plaintiff thinks there are lovers when going to dance halls, it is also a bit too much. Hu Die then continued to say that the defendant asked to terminate the engagement first, and my lawsuit with Lingbao was later. How can it be blamed on believing newspaper lies? The judge then asked Lawyer E on what day the letter of termination was sent. (E) At that time, the defendant saw what was published in the big newspaper (the three-day big newspaper) and entrusted me to send a letter to the plaintiff, advocating the termination of the engagement. My lawyer advised him not to overbelieve what the newspaper said. The defendant said that not only did the newspaper report it, but Zhou Jianyun of Star also said that the plaintiff had decided to terminate the engagement. Therefore, I specifically asked to send a letter first. My lawyer then wrote the letter on his behalf.

▲ Lin Xuehuai Denies Using Money Lin Xuehuai finally said, "What Ms. Hu said is all empty words. Since I was over ten years old, I have never been unemployed. Why would I use her allowance? The house she lived in before she became famous only cost 15 yuan a month, so there is no way she would have money to give me. If I needed her allowance, why would she marry a poor guy?" Lawyer Zhan then continued to state that the defendant's lawyer had just said that whoever's name was on the car registration owned the car, which was a big mistake. You must know that the car registration is available to everyone, so if that's the case, then the car drivers are all the owners. Besides, the cost of buying the car and the defendant's debts have all been proven. Lawyer E refuted, saying that the civil law has a clause on donations. Even if the cost of buying the car did not come from him, if the person who paid for it had already donated it to the defendant, it should not be recovered. Lawyer Zhan then refuted that the donor has the responsibility to provide proof that it was a gift and cannot rely on empty words.

Judge Zhou Strongly Urges Reconciliation At this time, it was 12:30 noon, and the judge then announced that the case would be adjourned to 9:00 AM on March 20 and also told Hu Die that it would be best to try to reconcile out of court. If there was a possibility, the lawyers of both parties could mediate. Otherwise, the court would rule according to the law and then announced the adjournment.

▲ The Shape of the Black Gold Ring The questions examined yesterday were purely the questions listed in the plaintiff's complaint. The defendant's counterclaim was not examined. However, there was a matter of returning the black gold ring in his counterclaim. It is said that the ring is worth four hundred gold. This ring was brought to the court by Lawyer Zhan yesterday. Because the counterclaim was not examined, it was not presented. According to those who saw the ring, the outside looks like nine-karat gold, with something inside that resembles a bullet in a hunting gun. However, it is not possible to say for sure whether it is black gold.

▲ The Process of Reconciliation Failure This newspaper reported yesterday that there was a trial reconciliation in the Hu-Lin termination case, which was true. The reason why both parties were still involved in court yesterday was that the defendant did not go to sign at that time, which led to the failure of the reconciliation. Here is a recap of the situation on that day. Lin had previously been introduced by Qiu Yuan of Wing On Company to meet with the plaintiff's representative, Lawyer Zhan, to express his willingness to reconcile and settle the debt. After several consultations, they were quite close and agreed to go to the lawyer's office at 1:30 PM the day before to sign a reconciliation agreement. At the same time, Zhan also arranged for Hu Die and her father to be there to sign. The agreement had a total of five articles, the content of which was roughly that both parties agreed to terminate the engagement, and neither party would interfere with the other's marriage in the future. Hu Die would return the engagement ring, and neither party would bring up the old matters, otherwise, they would be liable. The agreement had a total of four pages. In addition to each party holding one page, there were two pages stored with the witness, Mr. Zhou, and the certifying lawyer, Zhan Ji. After this agreement was written and agreed to by both parties, Hu first signed the cross on it. Lin then said that he had to go home and would come back at 5:00 PM to sign. However, by evening, Lin had not gone, so they met in court yesterday.

If it is still not enough, Huang's private property should also be considerable. For the debt amount of Gongfa Company, at least three-quarters can be repaid in the short term. As for the remaining number, it can also be cleared within a few years. It's just that there is no man in their house, and Chen Genwei falsely claims to be a sibling, but is actually committing adultery. For example, there is one instance:

When Chen Genwei was taking a bath, Zou Aizhen would also go to wash her face. When Chen had leftover porridge, Zou would eat it for him. At the same time, his maid, Zhou A'mei, also told me about it. Zhou A'mei was also indignant about it. In addition, many neighbors around also knew about it. Furthermore, she (Aizhen) gave birth to a child in December. I know that I had lived with her in May. How could she give birth to a child in only six months?

It is evident that it is an illegitimate child." Police Officer He Fenglin testified, "I am a police officer from the third precinct of the first district. When Tang went to report the adultery, I was at the bottom of the stairs and did not go up. Later, they brought Chen Genwei and Zou Aizhen up. and Zou Aizhen was wearing underwear. I was only dispatched

by the police chief. At the time of departure, I did not know what it was about. I only found out after arriving at Zou's house." Chen Genwei testified, "Zou Aizhen and I are foster siblings. Tang Huixuan and Zou Aizhen came from the United States one after the other. At that time, I was acting on internal orders to go to Beiping to negotiate construction matters. I was living in the back building of Zou's house. Tang wanted to use me

to facilitate his divorce from his wife. Therefore, he asked Le Zifang to persuade me to reconcile, but I refused." Zou Yuezhen testified, "Zou Aizhen is my sister, and Chen Genwei is my foster brother. He has always been in my house. Tang said,

'This is the woman,' and took her to the police station." Zou Aizhen testified, "I was sleeping when I heard my sister arguing with them, so I came out. Tang Huixuan said, 'This is the woman,' and then went to the police station." Last year, before Tang came home, three boxes arrived first.

Inside were all women's clothing. When I questioned him about it, he said that a friend had asked him to bring them. A few days later, Tang asked for a private divorce, but I did not agree. So he falsely accused me. Regarding the matter of raising the child, when I asked him for medical expenses, he said that raising a child was

fulfilling his obligation to the country and that he did not think it was anything special. Please consider his character to this extent." Tang Huixuan stated, "My ten years of savings are all tied up in her name. Now I have nothing to use," and presented a stack of pawn tickets. He added, "If Aizhen can break away from her relationship with Chen, the couple can reconcile." The judge said that further investigation was needed and adjourned the hearing. Furthermore, Tang Huixuan believed that the telegram urging him to return home was a deceitful scheme designed by a third party to falsely accuse him of the risk of escaping, so he declared that he would never leave Shanghai.

A Kidnapped Child Rescued in Meiyan Township, Wujiang

▲Only After Arriving in Shanghai Was It Discovered It Was Not Li's Son

▲Detectives Made Two Trips to Wujiang to Rescue

The four-year-old son of a Mr. Li, residing at No. 38 Anren Lane, Kangti Road, French Concession, was playing at the door with his nanny on the evening of February 15th when he was kidnapped by bandits and escaped. The victim immediately reported the case to the French Concession Police Department, requesting investigation and arrest. Subsequently, it was discovered that after abducting the child, the kidnappers had taken him to Meizhen Township in Wujiang County, Suzhou, to hide. The case was immediately reported to the Captain, and Chief Detective Lai'er, along with Chinese detectives Zhang Pingpu, Yang Shan, and others, were dispatched to Suzhou to collaborate with the patrol officers of the third district of the Water Police and the detectives of the fifteenth team of Wujiang to rush to Meizhen Township for a search. However, the kidnappers had already fled after hearing the news, and only the kidnapped child was rescued. In addition, a box cannon, two rifles, and three carbines were found in an abandoned coffin in a certain family's cemetery nearby. Later, the Chinese and Western detectives brought the child to Shanghai, and the victim confirmed that it was not Li's son. The police have now discovered that the rescued child is the son of a certain family in Gutazhen Township, Wujiang, who was also kidnapped by bandits. Therefore, Detective Yang Shan and others were dispatched for a second time to Suzhou, and then to Wujiang, to collaborate with the local water and land police detectives to search for Li's kidnapped child.

A Huge Stash of Silk Found in the Partition Wall of an Italian Hotel

▲The Italian Was Sentenced to Three Months in Prison and Fined 4,000 Taels

▲The Defendant Declared Dissatisfaction and Will Appeal

According to the "Great American Evening Post," regarding the major case of the theft of seventy-three bolts of silk from a certain shop at No. 1017 Jing'an Temple Road last month on the 29th, after the detectives arrested three Russian thieves, they recovered forty-five bolts of the original stolen goods inside the partition wall of the hotel established by the Italian Bin Du at No. 46 Bazilu Road. Subsequently, the Italian was sent to the Italian Consulate General and charged with receiving stolen goods. Yesterday (the 27th),

the court opened the trial in the afternoon. First, the Western detective stated that after arresting the three Russian thieves who committed the theft, he went to search the defendant's hotel and found the situation of finding forty-five bolts inside the partition wall. Currently, two Russians have been sentenced to 18 months in prison, one person to 20 months in prison, and another Russian was fined 1,000 yuan for mediating the sale of stolen goods. Next, the defendant was questioned and claimed that he did not know that the goods were stolen goods, so he dared to buy them. Then, the three Russians were summoned to testify about the defendant's situation of transporting goods to their residence. The judge then sentenced the defendant to three months in prison and ordered him to compensate the victim for the original price of 73 bolts of silk, which was 4,000 taels. The defendant declared in court that he was not satisfied and would appeal. He was then released on the original bail pending trial. It is said that after this case is appealed, it must be tried by a higher Italian court.

The Second Route of the Chinese Merchants' Public Bus Will Be Suspended Tomorrow

The Zhabei Chinese Merchants Public Bus Company originally had 26 buses, divided into three routes. The first route had 11 buses, running from Baoshan Road to Jiangwan; the second route had 4 buses, running from Qiujiang Road and North Sichuan Road to Xinzha Bridge; and the third route had 11 buses, running from Baoshan Road to Zhenru. Routes one and three saw prosperous business, but the second route had fewer passengers since it was opened on May 16th of the 18th year, and business failed to develop. From September 1st of the 18th year, the full route fare of 27 cents was changed to 21 cents. At that time, the route still extended east to North Sichuan Road and west to Hengfeng Bridge. On September 1st of the 19th year, the route was changed again to the west to Xinzha Bridge, in an attempt to attract more passengers. However, for several months, the number of passengers was still scarce, and business made no progress. The company's manager, Lei Zhaopeng, decided that from March 2nd, the second route of public buses would be completely suspended, and the reason for the suspension would be reported to the Municipal Public Works Bureau for record.

The Shanghai-Minhang Long-Distance Bus Increases Prices

▲The Full Route is 7 Jiao and 5 Fen

Since the Shanghai-Minhang-Nanzhe Long-Distance Bus Company added new buses and worked hard to reorganize, transportation has become more convenient, business has developed, and local merchants and residents have praised it unanimously. Recently, due to the soaring prices of oil and tires, and the continued increase in the prices of various parts, the ticket price revenue is not enough to maintain the current situation. It has been reported to the Municipal Public Works Bureau for approval, and the full route ticket price has been increased by 1 jiao and 1 fen. The bus ticket from Shanghai to Minhang is now 7 jiao and 5 fen, and each station along the route will increase prices separately according to the kilometer. It is reported that the company is scheduled to implement this today and has notified all stations to check accordingly.

The Wing On Company Savings Department is Reorganized into a Bank

The Savings Department operated by the Wing On Company was originally allocated a fund of one million yuan by the company. The business and accounting have always been independent, and the credit has been very good. In fact, it is no different from an independent bank, but because it has not been registered with the government, its legal status is not separate from the Wing On Company itself, which violates the suspicion that the store is also operating savings. A resolution has been made by Guo Le, Guo Biao, Guo Quan, Yang Huiting, Guo Shun, Ouyang Minqing, Du Zewen, Guo Linshuang, Guo Ruixiang, and others to completely separate the Savings Department from the Wing On Company to form an independent bank, which is named Wing On Commercial Savings Bank. The company's accounting consultant, Accountant Pan Xulun, has been entrusted to prepare the registration procedures so that the interests of each saver can be fully guaranteed in the future.

▲Two People Fined One Yuan Together

Ordinary men, women, and children saw the copper teeth fitted on their white teeth and thought they looked like gold teeth from afar, so they were eager to try them out to show off. Therefore, they rushed to have them fitted, and the stalls were extremely crowded with children, and business was not bad. Later, a teacher from a certain elementary school passed by and saw this and reported it to the Third District Police Station, saying that this kind of copper tooth, when placed in the mouth, was harmful to health, and if the children were not careful, they might swallow it, which would be life-threatening. The police station ordered the two men to be taken to the district. According to their confession, one was Zhang A'san, 43 years old, from Yancheng, and the other was Zhang A'rong, 37 years old, from Yancheng. They both claimed that they came to Shanghai to make a small living in this original way to make a living because their hometown was barren and they had no way to make a living. Madam Gao, the mother of Mr. Shen Lianfang, the former chairman of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, suddenly died in her Shanghai residence at the hour of Chou (1-3 AM) yesterday (the 28th), at the age of 83. The funeral will be held at the hour of Shen (3-5 PM) on March 2nd (that is, tomorrow). Madam Gao was kind and benevolent and was known for her charitable deeds. Upon hearing of her death, everyone deeply mourned.

Education News

This port

Municipal Executive Committee Sets Procedures for Establishing Municipal and District Education Associations

The Shanghai Special Municipality Party Headquarters' People's Training Committee, based on the People's Organizations Regulations and relevant laws concerning education associations, drafted a procedure for establishing Shanghai Municipal and District Education Associations, which was submitted to and approved by the 91st Standing Committee Meeting of the Municipal Executive Committee. The original text is transcribed below:

▲ Procedures for Establishing Shanghai Municipal and District Education Associations

1. To initiate the organization of a district education association, there must be at least twenty-eight representatives within that district who possess the membership qualifications stipulated in Article 16 of the Education Association Law. These representatives must jointly submit a letter of justification and the resumes of the initiators (resume forms can be obtained from the Municipal People's Training Committee), in duplicate, to the Municipal People's Training Committee for approval.

2. To initiate the organization of a municipal education association, the consent of more than half of the affiliated district education associations must be obtained, and representatives must be nominated. A letter of justification, in duplicate, must be submitted to the Municipal People's Training Committee for approval.

3. After receiving the application, the Municipal People's Training Committee will immediately send personnel for inspection. If the establishment is approved, the Municipal People's Training Committee will issue a permit and notify the Municipal Education Bureau for their record.

4. After receiving the Municipal People's Training Committee's approval, the initiators of the municipal or district education association should immediately send personnel to the Municipal People's Training Committee to collect the permit.

5. The municipal or district education association, having been approved for preparation, should nominate three to nine preparatory members to form a preparatory committee and report to the Municipal People's Training Committee and the Municipal Education Bureau for record.

6. The preparatory committee of the municipal or district education association should carve a seal with the name approved by the Municipal People's Training Committee, stating "Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Municipal (某某 District) Education Association," using regular script. The date of activation and a specimen of the seal should be reported for record.

7. The preparatory period for municipal and district education associations is limited to ten days after the preparatory committee is recorded. After preparations are completed, a draft constitution and a membership list (constitution and membership list paper can be obtained from the Municipal People's Training Committee) should be submitted to the Municipal People's Training Committee for review.

8. The constitution of the municipal or district education association should specify the following items: (1) Name, region, and association address; (2) Regulations for membership admission, withdrawal, and expulsion; (3) Number, duties, and election/removal procedures for officers; (4) Regulations regarding meetings; (5) Regulations regarding finances.

9. After the draft constitution and membership list of the municipal or district education association are approved by the Municipal People's Training Committee, a founding conference should be convened immediately, and the Municipal People's Training Committee and the Municipal Education Bureau should be requested to send personnel for guidance and supervision.

10. After the municipal or district education association is established, a list of important officers should be filled out, and any changes in the constitution and membership list should be reported to the Municipal People's Training Committee and the Municipal Education Bureau for record.

11. This procedure shall be implemented upon resolution by the Executive Committee of the Chinese Nationalist Party's Shanghai Special Municipality.

Municipal Education Bureau Punishes Schools in the Municipality That Abandoned the Lunar Calendar and Suspended Classes

The Municipal Education Bureau announced yesterday: "It has been found that this Bureau previously issued a notice and published an announcement in newspapers to all schools in the city, in accordance with the regulations for promoting the National Calendar New Year, stating that they must not take holidays from February 10th to the end of February without authorization. At the beginning of the Lunar New Year, this Bureau dispatched 43 staff members to conduct thorough investigations in various districts of municipal and registered private schools to determine whether classes were being held as usual for assessment purposes. According to the investigation reports, in the Huhang, Zhabei Special District, 7 private schools out of 166 schools investigated were found not to be holding classes. In the Qingpu District, 6 municipal schools and 1 registered private school were found not to be holding classes. These cases have been submitted to the 186th Bureau Affairs Meeting for deliberation and separate punishment. The principals of the following seven schools – Municipal Tangyan Elementary School, Jingnan Elementary School, Zhuyin Elementary School, Private Zhengfeng Middle School, Ningbo Fellow-Villagers Association First Elementary School, Shuguang Elementary School, and Yide Girls' Elementary School – were present at school, but classes could not be held due to the small number of students attending. The principals of these schools failed to effectively prevent this from happening; they should be severely reprimanded and instructed to forward the reprimand to teachers, staff, and students as a warning. The following seven schools – Municipal Guanlong Elementary School, Zhangtang Elementary School, Donggou Elementary School, Private Sijing Elementary School, Qunxian Girls' Elementary School, Qianjiang Elementary School, and Youde Elementary School – completely suspended classes, and the principals were also absent from school. This is a violation of the law. The salaries of all principals of the municipal schools will be reduced by one grade for one month, and the private school principals will be reprimanded and instructed to forward the reprimand to teachers, staff, and students as a warning. In addition to separate orders, this is a general announcement to all schools in the city for their information."

Municipal Education Bureau Forbids Villagers from Entering Temples to Worship Gods During the Lantern Festival

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau received reports from the municipal Guanqiao and Lingqiao Elementary Schools stating that, according to local customs, people would go to temples to worship gods during the Lunar Lantern Festival, and the school buildings of these schools are borrowed from temples. Therefore, classes could not be held as usual during that period, and they requested instructions on how to handle the situation. At a time when the National Calendar New Year is being promoted and superstitions are being broken, such erroneous practices should be prohibited. The Bureau reported the situation to the Public Security Bureau for handling. Subsequently, a reply was received, stating that all districts under their jurisdiction have been ordered to strictly prohibit such activities.

The Boy Scouts of China, Shanghai Municipal Council, will begin handling the registration of service personnel, boy scouts, and boy scout troops starting on March 1st. Unexpectedly, Zhen Ru Defeats Schutze

▲ Result: 3-1

The Whole Story of Lehua's Failed European Expedition

| An Uneven Cry from Englishman Li Silian |

Englishman Li Silian, a veteran of Shanghai football and also a famous referee, served as the football coach of Nanyang (now Jiaotong University) for many years and was the first trainer of the Chinese football team. He has now expressed his final opinion on the resolution of the amateur status of the Lehua Football Team by the Shanghai and Hong Kong Westerners' Football Clubs, which is recorded as follows:

▲ The Purpose of the Expedition is Just and Honorable

At the beginning of 1929, the public knew that the Lehua Athletic Association proposed organizing a football team to tour Europe and the United States in the autumn of 1930. First, they would visit various countries in continental Europe, as well as England and Scotland, and on their return journey, they might also visit Canada and the United States. The main purpose of this trip was to connect with and compete with the friendship of various countries, to give young players a good and beneficial journey, and to allow European and American countries to recognize the demeanor of new Chinese athletes, who could be on par with other countries. From this, it can be inferred that today's Chinese sports are not as poor and backward as they usually imagine.

▲ The Consultation in Europe is Extremely Satisfactory

In the summer of 1929, when Mr. Li Silian went to England, officials from the Lehua Athletic Association asked Mr. Li to contact Europe and England and report back to Shanghai to decide on the next steps. Mr. Li took advantage of his holidays in Europe to contact various sports associations and, before leaving England to return to Shanghai, personally discussed the Lehua trip to Europe with Sir Frederick Wall, the secretary of the English Football Association, who actually controls football movement worldwide. At that time, he obtained the oral approval of the Sir, and confirmed that Lehua's actions were within the scope of amateur sports. In addition, the Continental Association, which governs football movements in various countries in continental Europe, also promised to provide full support.

▲ The Expedition Sets Out, All Preparations are Made

After Mr. Li returned to China and told Lehua about the results of his consultation and the implementation strategy, which was fully adopted, it was scheduled to depart from Singapore in mid-August in order to arrive in Europe in the football season. First, Lehua went to Java and the South Pacific Islands to compete, in order to raise funds for the expedition to Europe and the United States, and to select players from Hong Kong, Singapore, and other ports in the South Pacific Islands to form an extremely strong team. Mr. Li would temporarily stay in Shanghai to communicate with Europe, and then go to Singapore by boat with Lehua to Europe.

▲ The Hong Kong Football Club Raises Trouble Without Reason

In mid-August 1930, when all matters were about to come to an end, the Hong Kong Football Club suddenly banned its Chinese players from participating in the expedition. The reason was that Lehua had lost its amateur status and had become a professional. A huge wave arose from this. The British Football Association sent a telegram to postpone the process and wait for the so-called professional evidence and letters from Hong Kong before making a decision. Everything was delayed, and the ambition of the expedition could not wait any longer. The entire Lehua army decided to return to Shanghai.

▲ Major Events are Handled Casually

After Lehua returned to Shanghai, the Shanghai Football Association had a meeting to organize a special committee to review Lehua's content and players' amateur qualifications. Five months later, until January 20, the Shanghai Football Association disclosed the resolution of the association in various newspapers. It should be noted that the association did not organize any special committees, but this important resolution seemed to be produced in the ordinary executive committee, and none of Lehua officials was invited to attend the meeting to state the facts, so the resolution was obtained in a camera. Before the resolution was disclosed, the China National Amateur Athletic Federation had already held a special committee to review everything and publicly recognized that Lehua still had amateur qualifications and had no professional behavior.

▲ The Shanghai Football Club Refuses to Explain

The Shanghai Football Association's resolution confused the public. With the consent of Lehua officials, Mr. Li formally wrote to the Westerners' Football Club asking it to explain the declaration and show evidence. Two weeks later, Mr. Li received a reply from the association stating that the results of the association's review had been made public and told him that there was no need to reply to this matter again. In other words, the Westerners' Club completely refused to answer the explanations requested by Mr. Li and Lehua.

▲ The Upper and Lower Organs Have Conflicting Views

On February 7, 1931 (this year), the North China Daily News published a message stating that the British Football Association had notified the Hong Kong Football Club that Cao Guicheng and Chen Guangyao of the South China Football Club and Lehua players were all qualified amateurs and had not committed any professional misconduct, and could still participate in all amateur games in the future. Now, the two national football governing bodies, such as the China National Amateur Athletic Federation and the British Football Association, have declared that Lehua is a non-professional athlete. How can the local authorities, such as the Shanghai and Hong Kong Football Clubs, impose the crime of becoming professional? On February 10, Mr. Li again wrote to the Shanghai Football Club, asking it to pay attention to the British Football Association's resolution, but to this day, Mr. Li has not received a single reply.

▲ Let the Public Judge the Merits and Demerits

Now, the Shanghai Football Club accuses Lehua of violating the amateur regulations of the British Football Association. However, the China Sports Association has declared that it has not committed any professional suspicions, and the British Football Association has expressed this later. I do not know if the Association can insist on this attitude. As for the other sections mentioned by the association, there is no point in defending them. However, Mr. Li and Lehua are eager for the public to understand the truth of the matter. Where are the merits and demerits? Can it be judged by the public, or by the Shanghai Football Club or the Lehua Football Team?

▲ Do Not Blame the Past, Strive for the Future

Mr. Li did not intend to resist the actions of the Shanghai Football Club, but for the sake of Lehua's reputation and status, and for the sake of the Chinese football team and players in the future, he had to make this statement. Mr. Li deeply felt that the soundness of Lehua's previous moral spirit should be rewarded with today's fairness, which would have a good influence on the country and the youth in the future, and is worthy of praise. Mr. Li's final contribution is that he hopes not to blame the past, strive for the future, unite as one, and express the spirit of the Chinese people, which should be the same on and off the field.

| Luo Haiguang, Chen Jiaqiu, and Chen Zhenhe Each Scored One Goal |

| Schutze's Failure is Due to Gu Tore's Calamity |

Yesterday, more than 6,000 spectators in the Shen Garden were sincerely delighted, and saw the athletes of Zhen Ru show their skills and talents, scoring one goal, two goals, and three goals, and defeating the Schutze army, and returning triumphantly with a result of three to one. The chief hegemon in Group A of the Westerners' Club was actually defeated by the students of Zhen Ru. Such things are unpredictable in the world. However, Zhen Ru did take the upper hand with its superior technology, and the enemy could only sigh and admit defeat.

▲ The Heroes of the Two Teams... Lining Up Against Each Other

The strength of Zhen Ru's new formation is twice that of the previous one. Yesterday's defeat of the strong enemy was not necessarily due to its strength. The absence of the center forward caused some concern at first. Fortunately, the center back line was solid and reliable, and then the front and rear parts were able to cope with ease. The performance of the whole army was excellent, but the goalkeeper Xie Quanhe and the left winger Chen Bingxiang were slightly worse. Schutze's center back George was powerful in the first half, but cramped in one side in the second half. The front and back were like two people. The ultimate failure was due to the two mistakes of inside guard Gu Tore.

▲ Zhen Ru Team

Xie Quanhe, Feng Yunyou, Jiang Shanqing, Liang Shutang, Zhuang Shihong, Lin Songfa, Chen Bingxiang, Luo Haiguang, Chen Jiaqiu, Chen Zhenhe, Mei Hongbao

▲ Schutze

Man Shishi, James, Gu Tore, Han Ladie, George, Nan Er, Wilson, Greyham, Brandt, Pan Erden, Che Erden

▲ The Forwards Gain Momentum... The Base Camp is Lost

Zhen Ru fiercely pounced against the wind, advancing without retreating. Zhuang's center back sent and received twice, creating endless waves. The Schutze army invaded, taking advantage of the second penalty from Lin and Zhuang, and went deep into the territory. The right inside shot, and the ball bounced to the rear. Mei Hongbao raised his troops on the right border, and Chen Zhenhe and Luo Haiguang echoed each other. The opposing goalkeeper had to go out twice to seize the ball to be safe. Twelve minutes of time had passed, and the right winger Che Erden shot. The goalkeeper Xie bent down to lift the ball, but the Flying General Pan Erden descended from the sky and kicked it into the net from the goalkeeper's hand. Xie was quick to respond and it was not difficult to turn danger into safety.

▲ The Whole Army Rises... And Takes Down the Fortress in One Go

After Schutze scored a goal, there was another period of excitement. Fortunately, Xie, the goalkeeper, had made a decision early and was rescued in time. The entire Zhen Ru army rose, and Luo Haiguang rushed out in front, taking the lead. Making feints to the east and attacking in the west, he crossed the door obliquely. Jiang and Feng were far away to respond. The two generals, Chen and Mei, advanced side by side. The ball was passed to the center. Luo Haiguang turned it over to the left. Chen Bingxiang was in the middle and offside. Chen Luo advanced again, but it was invalid offside. Zhen Ru launched three major attacks. The ball initially invaded from the right, and then turned to the center. Luo Haiguang unexpectedly shot fiercely at the door. The ball came out like an arrow and hit the net. Chen Zhenhe singled out the horse and mistakenly hit the goalkeeper's hand and was blocked by it. Chen Bingxiang once again went deep into the lone army and shot the goalpost. The rebounding ball was greeted by Chen Zhenhe's head and was caught by the goalkeeper again. In the first half, one-on-one, it was difficult to determine the outcome.

▲ The Head Turned Against... And Flew Into the Net

Not long after the start of the second half, Zhen Ru Haihongbao made a stunning move, and made the first attempt to explore the door. A ball flew to the corner of the door, and the goalkeeper jumped up and swooped out. The Schutze army was like a one-word formation, and the five tigers advanced in parallel. The right came and was blocked by Jiang, and the left was struck by the goalkeeper. As the enemy's momentum retreated, Zhen Ru once again raised Chen Zhenhe to lead the three armies, hitting the goal post three times before and after, just like coming out of the same mold. There was a general saying that the god was here, and there were no taboos. Fifteen minutes later, Chen's center forward Jiaqiu was about thirty yards away, suddenly raised his foot to attack. It happened that the inside guard Gu Tore's head turned against the sky, touched the back of his head, and flew towards the door. The goalkeeper was distraught and at a loss. The ball kicked on the top, flew into the net with the fake degree guard. It was unexpected and the audience was amazed. At that time, Zhen Ru took the lead with two to one.

▲ A Penalty Kick... A Great Success

After the two teams got closer, most of the time was spent going back and forth. If so, for fifteen minutes, the five generals of Zhen Ru were also in high spirits. Luo Hai greeted him and topped the ball forward. Chen Bingxiang chased after the shadow, and collided with the guard Ge Tore. The ball hit Ge's arm, and the penalty was twelve yards. Chen Zhenhe assumed the mission of the whole army, presided over the execution, and hit the net with a bang. The Schutze army suffered two misfortunes, and the center forward retired again, and ten people responded to the battle, leading the troops out of the city to fight back. Zhen Ru resisted and made more offensives, but the offside was invalid. As a result, three to one, Zhen Ru won. The referee was Li Te.

Free Talk 112

World Anecdotes · Sea · Guest

▲ A large educational club in London, England. Membership is extremely limited. If someone wants to join, they must wait ten years for a vacancy to become available.

▲ Italy has very little water power throughout the country. However, they are very good at utilizing lake and river water to increase electricity supply, greatly reducing coal imports.

▲ Among the Indians of South America, a new ethnic group has been discovered. Their skin is completely red. They have no government, no religion. The whole tribe is harmonious, without any struggles or worries.

▲ There is a movie in the United States called "Four Seasons." It is entirely a study of natural history throughout the year, increasing the audience's knowledge of nature. It took three years to produce.

▲ Many ancient coins were found in the belly of a bull slaughtered in a slaughterhouse in England. Among them were coins from the time of King Charles II, which are extremely valuable.

▲ Since the European War, Germany has lost many colonies. Therefore, it has issued various commemorative stamps to mourn the loss of the motherland's colonies. One of them has a thick black border and depicts a national flag, resembling a flag at half-mast.

▲ Two monkeys in the London Zoo are adept at stealing. Once, during a bank holiday, they stole a tourist's purse, containing six small mirrors, a veil, a leather wallet, three gloves, a handkerchief, and a gold watch chain, and a pipe.

▲ Many businessmen in the United States are obsessed with fate. Therefore, they often prepare a charm. Recently, many people have been using foreign dolls as charms.

Chinese Students Studying in Western Schools, Tears of America

I have often heard people say that Chinese people studying in schools founded by Westerners are most easily corrupted by Westerners. The result is that they are willing to submit to Westerners. I say, that's not true. Those who study in Western schools often work hard with international ideas, often wanting to win honor for their country.

My cousin, Mr. Cheng, studied at a public school. The school was founded by the Public Works Bureau. Although the students are all Chinese, the teachers, except for those who teach Chinese, are all Westerners. He once told me something: One day, an English teacher, a certain Englishman, asked the students to write an English paper with the topic "Chinese Pirates." The students knew that the teacher wanted to humiliate the Chinese with this, so the meaning of the articles they wrote all said, "Pirates are a kind of thief who rob and plunder in the sea in gangs. There are the most Englishmen in the world who are pirates. Therefore, great robberies often occur in the Atlantic Ocean along Europe. Even the Spanish naval fleet did not dare to sail in this area. (In 1833, the Spanish navy was the best in the world. Later, Spain and England fell out and fought a great battle in the Atlantic Ocean. The British army was defeated. The Spanish army pursued them and encountered British pirates on the way. The pirates defeated the Spanish army and seized countless military equipment and ships. The Spanish army heard about the British pirates, and they were all terrified. The British navy relied on it to become the dominant force in the world.) Our country has no pirates. It is because European and American movies are imported. The movies all talk about European and American pirates. Our people follow suit, so pirates also occur." The Western teacher was furious after reading it and deleted it all and sent it down. The students were all angry and tore it up. So the classroom was full of flying paper, which was quite a sight.

A Record of Two Red Doctors in Hongkou · · Knight

Xu Xiaopu of Wuchang Road specializes in pediatrics. Since his residence was rebuilt, it has become even more magnificent and resplendent. He sees patients every day, always around 180, and is very busy. A friend took his son to see him the other day. It was only a second or two away from the scheduled time. Just as he was reaching into his pocket to get the money, the registration clerk urged him, saying, "Hurry, hurry! Otherwise, once the bell rings, you will have to pay four dollars and four cents twice as much." His self-worth is so high.

Zhu Ziyun of Zhoujiazui's business is no less than Xu's, but his fee is one dollar less. Whenever you call a rickshaw, just tell them "Dr. Zhu Ziyun," and most people know where it is. Since the second time he was unbound, the precautions have been strict. He hired a bailiff from the Yamen and installed three iron gates, which are closed immediately upon entry. Treating patients is no different from treating serious prisoners, but it is also a way to prevent problems before they occur.

There was another day when a drawing teacher, Mr. Smith, asked the students to draw a map of China and draw other things on the map to embellish it. A student finished drawing and drew a large merchant ship, more than ten stories high, with our national flag hanging on it, majestic and awe-inspiring, sailing in the East China Sea. Mr. Smith saw it and said to the student, "China does not have this kind of merchant ship. Only England has this kind of merchant ship in the world." So he forced the student to change the national flag to the British flag. The student had no choice but to erase it with an eraser several times and draw a small sampan with the British flag hanging on it. Mr. Smith could do nothing about it.

Interesting Snippets from the Opening of the "Snow Butterfly" Divorce Case, Can Rong

Since the movie stars Lin Xuehuai and Hu Die had disagreements, they filed a lawsuit in court for the dissolution of their marriage contract and the recovery of debts. People in the society are paying close attention. The 28th of this month was the date of the first trial. On that day, all the newspapers published the details of the case early. Therefore, hundreds of people went to the Provisional Court to listen in. Interesting things arose from this. ▲ Lin Jim is excited. The protagonist of the silent love case, Lin Jim, arrived at 8:00 in the morning. He inquired about the opening of the court hearing. Suffering from his inability to speak, he frequently made gestures and used a pen to communicate. He bumped into things everywhere, his expression very excited.

▲ Reporters are sleepy-eyed. Most reporters go to bed at 3:00 or 4:00 every morning, and this case happened to be tried at 9:00 in the morning. They probably didn't get enough sleep. However, this case is a sensational divorce case, and the society is paying close attention. They had to abandon their warm beds and attend to record. Their sleepy eyes are quite pitiful. Some reporters were so afraid of not being able to wake up early for this case that they didn't sleep all night. It was also hard.

▲ Temporary change of court. At 9:00, more than 200 people arrived to listen in. This case was a civil case and was originally scheduled to be tried in the ninth court. However, the ninth court only had seating for more than 30 listeners. Therefore, it was moved to the third criminal court because it could accommodate more listeners.

▲ Invite reporters to smoke red pills. After the news of the court change spread, the listeners all rushed into the third court. However, the court was still trying a case of private smuggling and smoking of red pills. The exhibits in the case were all smoking lamps, smoking pipes, and red pills. After the trial, all these exhibits were moved to the lawyer's seat. At that time, because the audience was crowded, the news reporters were already sitting on the lawyer's seat. Therefore, so many smoking tools were displayed in front of them, as if pitying the reporters for getting up early and lacking energy, inviting them to take a puff to refresh themselves.

▲ Waiting for the judge. The judge presiding over this case was Mr. Zhou Renda. Because the cases in the ninth civil court had not been tried, the court did not open until around 11:00. The listeners were already overcrowded and had been waiting for the judge for a long time, which was very frustrating. People continued to arrive in an endless stream. At that time, two Westerners stood behind the judge's seat and bowed to the crowd to elicit laughter. Their facial expressions and figures were very similar to those of Keystone.

▲ Lin Xuehuai is willing to do anything. Hu Die testified that Lin Xuehuai used to treat me very well. He was willing to do anything for me, even things that servants were unwilling to do... The meaning was profound. The listeners roared with laughter.

▲ Competing to take photos. In order to increase the interest of the news, each newspaper specially sent a photographer to take photos of the parties involved. Some took photos secretly, some requested them, and some pulled them hard. The parties involved were very busy, and the listeners followed and chased after them, like a collapsing torrent. It was truly a spectacle.

New Embellishments to Wuxi Park, He Tianjian

Every year, people in Wuxi take the park as the central point for recreation. Although the lunar calendar has been abolished, the custom still exists. Therefore, recently, the people playing in the park are still shoulder to shoulder, like a flock of birds. Among them, the most noteworthy new embellishments are Mr. Wu Zhilao's long couplet in the Tonggeng Hall and the artisticization of the Wuxi Grand Theater.

▲ The humor of Wu Zhilao's calligraphy couplet. The Tonggeng Hall was built by Mr. Cao Zhangheng and other elders at their own expense as a memorial to their common age. At the end of the abolished lunar year, when Mr. Wu Zhilao was in Wuxi, Cao Zhang and Mr. Wu were old friends. He asked Mr. Wu to write a couplet for the Tonggeng Hall. Mr. Wu agreed. However, after arranging the ink, Mr. Wu suddenly disappeared. Everyone thought that he did not want to write. Unexpectedly, after a few days, a postman came and delivered a letter, which turned out to be a couplet paper of one zhang. Looking at the inscription, the three characters "Wu Jingheng" were clearly visible. Everyone was disappointed but got this in the end, and they all praised it. The characters written were in seal script. The upper couplet said, "Talent can carve dragons, skills excel in embroidery tigers." The lower couplet said, "Strength is used to catch rabbits, wisdom holds spiritual snakes." There was also a postscript, but I don't remember it anymore. The original character for snake was 〇, which is an ancient character. Those who read it all mistook it for another character, or some even didn't recognize it. This shows the humor of this old man.

▲ The artisticization of the Wuxi Grand Theater. The Wuxi Grand Theater was founded by Mr. Wu Guanli. The architecture imitates the latest European style, covering more than one mu of land. It is located in the northwest corner of the park. It is equipped with a retractable roof and has complete equipment. The seats are wide and comfortable, without any crowding. The films ordered are all valuable films from Central Europe. The walls at the entrance are painted with lyrical goddesses, the work of artists Xing Zhonglian and Tang Xuandao. There are seven goddesses in the whole picture, all lifelike. This treasure is only seen in movie theaters. The grand opening ceremony of the theater was held on the first day of the abolished lunar calendar. Movie star Ms. Hu Die and Mr. Zhou Jun Jianyun were invited from Shanghai to participate in Wuxi. Ms. Hu was also invited to unveil the theater. Mr. Zhou called it a model movie theater in the interior. On that day, no less than thousands of people visited, which was also a grand occasion.

One Page of Dog Judging Scripture, Sick 〇

My friend Mr. Li has been teaching in a private school for ten years. Recently, he saw that his profession would eventually be eliminated, so he switched to studying medicine. He has also been studying for many years and has gained quite a lot of experience. He once borrowed several books on prescriptions from me and copied them by hand. Unfortunately, he died of illness last autumn. His family returned the borrowed books to me. When I checked them, there was a page of dog judging scripture clipped in them. I don't know where he copied it from. I am recording it for the Free Talk, just for the world's researchers who have a passion for Han Lu and Song Que.

Enter the door to the east, exit the door as a dragon. Enter the door to the west, exit the door as a maggot. (Note) Entering the door to the east means that the tail curves to the east. Entering the door to the west means that the tail curves to the west. Like a dragon or a maggot, the difference between good and bad is as great as heaven and earth.

Four feet high, thieves flee at the sight of the master. Four feet low, chasing rabbits in the wilderness is as fast as flying. (Note) High and low mean too high and too low. They are all strange appearances. Guarding the house and hunting, each is suitable for its use.

Two eyes blue, no one in the southern and northern villages can compare. Two eyes yellow, busy stealing food from the eastern and western families. (Note) Pure blue dog eyes are also a strange appearance, so they are fierce. Yellow eyes are inferior breeds.

Jade children are produced in Jiangnan, black dragons are produced in Jiangbei. It is rare to see them in different places. If you see them, they must be brave and heroic. (Note) Pure white is called jade children, pure black is called black dragons. Black dragons are common in Jiangbei, and jade children are often seen in Jiangnan. If they are produced in different places, there is no doubt that they are the leaders of their race.

If there is a golden lion yellow dog at home, there is no need to guard the front and back doors. If there is a peach blossom spotted dog at home, the kitchen will ring with knives every day. (Note) Golden lion yellow is a golden yellow lion dog. They are good at guarding the house. Peach blossom spots are white with spots, like peach blossoms. They are excellent hunting dogs, and they will ring with knives every day because of the game they bring back to be slaughtered.

Facial Assurance, Qiu Shui

▲ A Recent Interesting Story in an American Court According to American communications, in a certain place in Illinois, a female typist from a certain company drove her car from home to the company one morning to work. Because the car's speed was too high, she was stopped by the traffic police, who intended to fine her ten dollars. The woman had no way to pay, so she was arrested and taken to court. The judge presiding over the case saw that the woman was graceful and charming. He fell in love with her and released her. He allowed her to pay the fine tomorrow and did not detain her. He said, "Such a beautiful face is more than enough to guarantee ten dollars." It is also an interesting story. Therefore, I recorded it for everyone's amusement.

Eastward Travel Correspondence (27), Wu Xiaohou

The Tokyo Japan-China Association. The Tokyo Japan-China Association was initiated by Baron Shibusawa in April of the seventh year of Taisho (1918) with like-minded people. Its initial fund was composed of the remaining money from the Association of Students Studying in Japan, amounting to more than 37,500 yen, and 10,000 yen donated by Mr. Naito Hisakazu. The association's business was initially to guide Chinese students studying in Japan in selecting schools, transferring schools, providing dormitories, and introducing them to internships in banks, companies, factories, and stores. The first president was Mr. Komatsubara Eitaro. The directors were Mr. Naito Hisakazu, Mr. Yamamoto Jotaro, Mr. Shiraiwa Ryuhei, and Mr. Hamano Torakichi. Mr. Hamano Torakichi was also appointed as the permanent director. Baron Shibusawa, along with Viscount Kiyoura, Viscount Okabe, Baron Yamakawa, Baron Kondo, Baron Kaita, Mr. Tagawa Miharu, Mr. Toyokawa Ryohei, and Mr. Eto, served as advisors to the association. In addition, faculty members from the Imperial University and various public and private higher vocational schools, as well as officials from the three ministries of Education, Agriculture and Commerce, and Foreign Affairs (i.e., the three departments of Education, Agriculture and Commerce, and Foreign Affairs), and other famous figures from the government and the public were appointed as councilors. As a result, the foundation of the association was established, and its affairs grew more prosperous day by day. In October of the same year, the First Chinese Society was established. By July of the ninth year of Taisho (1920), the Mitsubishi Mitsui Company, the Yokohama Specie Bank, the Sumitomo Bank, and the Taiwan Bank, as well as Mr. Inoue Junnosuke and Mr. Kimura Seishiro, jointly donated 115,000 yen, and the Second Chinese Dormitory was established. In May of the tenth year of Taisho (1921), the Ministry of Education again subsidized 150,000 yen from the national treasury's petition fund. In June of the same year, it was formally reorganized and registered as a public interest foundation. In July of the same year, it purchased more than 220 tsubo of land at No. 15 Sakuma-cho, Kanda-ku, Tokyo, and built two-story and three-story buildings, each occupying half of the land (i.e., two-story and three-story buildings). This is the current association building. The current president is Marquis Hosokawa Moritatsu, who also serves as the principal of Tokyo Higher Preparatory School. The permanent director is Mr. Yamai Kakutaro. Mr. Hosokawa does not often attend the association, but his name is used for all external introductions and official documents. This is because Japan is an enlightened autocratic country and has not yet shaken off the feudal class ideology. It is more convenient to use the name of a marquis externally. Mr. Yamai, on the other hand, comes to the association every morning and leaves only at night. He is extremely kind and simple. When international organizations or commissioners come to Japan to visit, the association not only introduces them to accommodation and meals, but also sends a person in charge or other staff to accompany them during the visit, taking responsibility for guidance and interpretation. This is completely voluntary. When the reporter was investigating in Tokyo, although he could communicate in English or by writing Chinese characters (most people in the Japanese middle class and above are proficient in Chinese and familiar with English), he still felt inconvenienced. Fortunately, the association initially sent Mr. Uchida Takeo to accompany him, and then sent Mr. Okada Hisashi (Okada's father, Okada Yumin, lived in China for 30 years and is said to have a historical relationship with this newspaper, Shen Bao) to Yokohama. The convenience was great. As for the Chinese people, their criticism of the association is that it puts on a false show of hospitality to international investigators and that it does not come from sincerity but is pretentious and worthless. However, in all fairness, the association can sincerely guide and assist Chinese investigators and new students going to Japan (from the opening of the association to the end of Showa 1 (1926), the association subsidized expenses for more than 180 government-funded students from various provinces of China who were unable to continue their studies due to domestic wars or other obstacles that interrupted their funding. The provinces were Hunan, Jiangxi, Anhui, Sichuan, Hubei, Jiangsu, Guizhou, Fujian, Shaanxi, Henan, and Shanxi. The introduction of everything is also quite commendable.

Cotton Yarn: The Yarn Market Declines

The yarn market has turned weak, with a significant downward trend. Recent fluctuations have been rapid and substantial, causing considerable concern. This is mainly due to the continuous decline in overseas cotton yarn conditions over the past two days and the softer gold prices, along with the easing exchange rates. Market demand for spot yarn has been met for the next few days, and there are currently no expectations for significant development in the near future. The price of marked yarn has reached around 180 taels, showing instability. Due to these various factors, even slight negative news triggers market changes. However, based on raw material costs, factories are unable to profit, except for some manufacturers who purchased at lower prices and can still profit from the price difference with current cotton prices. Therefore, some have engaged in hedging. However, a major manufacturer is reportedly absorbing large quantities, with substantial contract volumes.
